Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	There is also a method such that you make three or four cauteries, lining them up according to the length of the mouse's body, following the shape of the liver cautery we mentioned earlier.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	And do not rush your hand for the entire cautery; let the patient often lie on his back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	And another method of cauterization is to heat the cautery which has two threads, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	And lift the heart which is located at the breast, where the edge of the patient's coat comes towards the left; and let the elevation by which you lift the heart be according to the heart, according to the length of the body, and let the cautery be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	Then put in the two burning threads until the heart is pierced on the other side; then pull out the cautery, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you wish, cauterize with all of the cautery having three threads.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has thrown off corruption for a long time, it is better than the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	Of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery should not be used on someone with dropsy except in the manner called "ascites.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then you must make four cauteries around the throat, one on the stomach, one on the liver, and one on the breast, and two behind the back on the spine, and one near the nipple.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	And let the cautery be held close to the point of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cautery open for a long time to throw out corruption, and do not neglect the care of the patient after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	And healing would hasten, and both intentions will be together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cautery for the belly is the one we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And that for the back be olive-shaped, according to what has been placed here before.
de l’enfleure des piez	Of the inflammation of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical, and are full of yellow water, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go too deep in by force, lest you spill out the yellow water, and let the cautery be according to this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Then make two cauteries on each leg at the point of the shinbone.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And let the cautery be long, one under the knee in front and the other behind, in the middle of the thigh.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	And let cauteries burn unchecked without being treated, until the boil discharges.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After treating other wounds as we have described.
de la menoison	Of epilepsy
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When coldness and moisture cause problems in the stomach, rendering the retaining and digestive powers of the stomach and intestines powerless, so that they cannot be cured by any remedies;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	And you see the patient suffering greatly and having strong virtues, then perform a great cautery on the stomach according to what is written earlier about the cautery of the stomach.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And four small cauteries around the navel like a small key-cautery, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see moisture abounding and the patient suffering greatly, then make one cautery on the point of the chin, one cautery on each ear, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one; for treatment is helpful when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are in the fundament, one or more, and are old with thick cold moist corrupt humors, and have been treated by division as we have said but there is no improvement, then perform cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three on the spine of the back, one directly below the shoulder-blades in a triangular pattern, and two below the navel.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	If you think his stomach is cold and the flesh not cooked, and you see the face swelling, then apply one large fire cautery on the stomach as mentioned before, another on the liver, and another on the spleen using a pointed cautery.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery remain for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating it, heal it until it is clean.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of the fleshy growth called "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you grasp the boil, first heat the cautery that resembles a razor, and then place it completely burning on that grasped boil;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	And let your hand remain there until the cautery reaches the root of the vein where blood flows.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there are many boils, cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	afterwards, treat them with healing ointments until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you cauterize with a large cautery on boils, it will be more helpful.
de plaie mal curee	Of poorly-treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	If the patient cannot endure incision or opening, which we will discuss in its proper place, then there comes such a disease that can only be cured by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a fistula comes to someone and it is inflamed and emits corruption and corrupt moistures, you should prove it with a thin probe entirely throughout its length, and make sure that you know the entire length of the probe.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	Then heat the cautery that resembles a razor, and insert it into the fistula according to how much tent is inside it, and recommence with the cautery until the rotted and corrupted flesh is burned, once, or twice, or three times depending on what is needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And guard against burning the nerves that are nearby, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes into the body of the bladder or intestines, beware of this place; and do not perform cautery except in a fleshy area; consider that it is not passing.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treating the place until it is clean, and if the wound is healed, and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the place is entirely healthy.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the matter is not removed, know that the place is putrefied, and the bone is rotting at its core.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And thus as one of those things which we will say in their place.
de la maladie des reins	de la maladie dels rengs (Occitan)
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold comes to the kidneys, and there is great windiness, and no sign of menstruation appears, then you must perform cautery on the kidneys on either side with the clavicle cautery that we have spoken of before.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize it midway, there will be three cauteries in a row.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	And when the bladder is weak and cold due to moisture so that the patient retains urine, then make two cauteries on each side above the bladder where the pubic hairs begin, each cautery being as long as a hazelnut.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	And make one cautery behind the back, or two if needed.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	And let the cauteries be shaped like a crow's foot according to the shape mentioned above.
de la marris	Of the womb
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the womb is cold and moist, preventing conception, and the flowers are corrupted with late terminations;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	And when they do come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	Then it is necessary to make three cauteries around the pudendum as we have said regarding the bladder cautery, and two cauteries behind the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	And let the cauteries be shaped like a crow's foot, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hair
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When viscous moisture descends to the box of the hip joint, causing it to move from its place, the sign is that one thigh appears longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	And the location of the joint's departure is found, so you should cauterize the patient around the hip socket with an iron cautery shaped like a circle, and mark around the socket in front of where it turns, so that the socket lies within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	And let the cauteries be such as those used for cauterizing the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauteries are not available, then make three large olive-shaped ones; let the cauteries be as long as all the fingers.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And apply the treatment until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of pain in the hair
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the hip socket due to coldness and dampness, and despite being treated according to what we have said earlier, the patient is not cured, and the disease is chronic:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then it is necessary for you to purge the patient of thick humors using foul-tasting pills or other similar good pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After that, perform the cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	And there are two ways to perform the cautery:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	That is, using burning medicines together, or fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery has many methods, one of which is:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	Thus: cauterize over the haunch bone with three triangular cauteries in this shape, and make them deep and wide. Leave a space of two fingers between each cautery; let the cauteries be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Sometimes, one cauterizes in the middle on top of the haunch bone, resulting in four cauteries arranged like this:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish to do so, cauterize along the circular line we mentioned earlier for dislocating the haunch;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But do it in such a way that the circle contains the entire haunch, and all the fat around the heart is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the manner that is done in sciatica, when the pain holds in the thigh and does not reach to the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes down to the thigh and the leg, apply two cauteries where the patient feels the pain, and one cautery above the ankle on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	And let the cautery be made of steel, and let the thickness of the heart be burned.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the patient feels that the pain extends down to two fingers from the foot or close by, cauterize there three points or four with the cautery called 'points'.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if more is needed, do likewise.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if it seems that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, apply a circular cautery with great care in all your cauteries, ensuring you do not burn too deeply and damage the nerves and large arteries, causing further harm to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who performed a fire cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they left it until the leg became entirely swollen, and the foot likewise, and it was pierced and corrupted throughout.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach remedy that caused death
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, perform a cautery on one and on the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	The wise men say in the cautery for the haunch that it should be made of iron and be as thick at the tip as a goose quill or slightly less, and have spaces between each other, with one space equal to the thickness of a barley grain.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	And let the tweezers be made of two parts, and also like tongs, with one handle made of iron.
et c’est li forme:	And this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And it should be heated until it is all red-hot and glowing, then place it on the box of the sick person's hair, and turn it towards the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize once with one cautery, and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	And then make an emplaster of butter, and let the wound remain open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treating it with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we refrain from using this cautery because of its intense heat, and few people use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	nevertheless, those who can endure it are benefited by good cauteries.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of burning medicine is this: you should make an instrument with tweezers, into which the edge of the door descends, and it should be made of bronze or iron on one side, long enough for its width, and at the top there are two noses, each with the thickness of a finger between them;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	And let them be opened wide and above, and join together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Next, place the box of the comb upon the sick person lying on their healthy side, and then press your hand firmly upon the box of the comb;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	Next, place between the two circles of hot iron, heated in the fire for one hour, and let the patient endure its warmth and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it finds therein a biting like that of fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the biting has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and remove the hot comb, leaving it on for three days, and apply butter until the blackness of the scorch is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	And leave it on for three more days until corruption appears;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be the final aid after treatment with ointments, until he is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make one instrument that draws blood according to what you did for the comb.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is the method of hot cautery, which I have written about in my treatise on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and live lime, an equal amount of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	If there is a small hole there, then let the point of a razor enter it;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place thereupon another pot well stoppered, and put upon it alkali and warm water, until you have two pots full of the powders which you can easily grasp with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it thus until hot water and liquid descend into the well-stopped pot, then take all that water and pour it upon hot alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very hot and ready for use in many medical operations and cauteries of other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs the work of fire and has other medicines with which one can cauterize the hair well, such as pitch and honey of almonds and hot water with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure where a man was healed from the pain of his hair and sciatic vein, and he praised it greatly, saying that no other treatment was used, and he was healed at once when this cure was performed, as told hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And thus you should take some fresh and dry verdigris [copper(II) acetate], grind it well with a bit of fat, and apply it on the thigh, knee, and calf where the pain resides, and bind it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And leave it for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter a bath until his body is a little warmed up, and lay him in bed, and the pain will all go away and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such cauteries except after evacuating blood from the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's bile, it helps greatly;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And this is how the cautery should be made.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen, grease it with old oil, and place it on the depression between the big toe of the foot and the one called the 'fossicle'.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry goat bile and heating it on fire until it becomes charcoal, you should place it on wool and let it cool.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And repeat this process again until you think by sight that the heat reaches the thigh and the pain ceases.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And this type of cautery is called 'goat's cautery'.
de la dolor dou dos	**of the pain in the back**
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or impact or excessive bleeding, or from similar matter spread coldly, in none of these cases does fire cautery help except for that which comes from the infusing of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary that after the patient has been relieved with fetid pills or similar ones, you perform three rows of cauteries marked with ash on their back where the pain resides, and in each row five or more cauteries according to the strength and amount that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And let the cautery be made according to the cautery called 'poins';
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	And if you see, make 3 or 4 cauteries on the median cautery of the shoulder in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Often this disease comes to small children, and the sign of its onset is that they have short breath when they stand up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you will find on the lower spine of the back, near the appearance that comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and wish to cure it, cauterize with the cautery of a cell according to this shape:
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cauterizing iron grips evenly each part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish to do so, cauterize around the spine at intervals of two or three lines, with the points close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Then cleanse the wound until it is sound according to what we have said, and make sure you do not apply cautery in a place where there is an abscess near a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	de la dolor des jointes
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pains in the joints are caused by moistures that spread throughout each limb of the body, and when pain comes into the feet, which physicians properly call 'podagra,' and when it is caused by coldness and cannot be cured by medications, then it should be treated with cauteries in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make many cauteries around the ankle joint, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to prick the surface of the foot, perform cautery with the cautery called "the point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains reach the knees and other joints, which happens often, make 3 or 4 cauteries on each knee, olive-shaped on both sides.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need more, then do more, but keep your hand steady until the brand of the heart's blade is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, then administer the cautery that we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then make punctures around the fistula two lines away.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there remains no pain at the base, then make punctures on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if pains reach to the elbows or shoulders, then cauterize each part, and have the patient keep a good regimen and take medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	But if you provide good care and purge phlegm, it will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	"Treatment for a broken nose:"
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture comes to the joints, and the bowels descend to the thighs, and it is recent, then you must ensure that when you see him being treated, he does not eat on that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	And let him use things that relieve the belly, so that the wind descends from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	Then have him sit on his back between your hands, and tell him to pull his ankle until the bowels are restored, and then bind them at your two elbows, and press firmly below the rupture on the bone of the wrist, and that is one sign that should resemble half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the cautery of which this is the shape
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it is white and casts shadows
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the intestines to their place.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	And the minister must hold his hand so that they do not slip backwards.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And open the patient's thighs widely, and place a cushion and a servant beneath them, and another serving the hands that hold him.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery on the sign with all your strength, holding it with your right hand and pushing until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, then begin again with even greater force until you feel the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	And be careful that the intestines do not slip out while applying the cautery
que tu ne le brulasses;	That you do not burn yourself
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	And that by this the patient does not die or suffer some other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	The cauteries for children should be thin according to their size, and those for large individuals should also be proportionately large.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, treat the wound from the cautery with butter until the burn is healed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After treating other wounds until they are sound, let the patient lie on their back for 40 days so that the wound is properly healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary to let his ligatures remain loose for a long time, so that his bowels do not protrude when he gets up from bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, give him a well-made bandage, and let him wear it for another 40 days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and have good rest, so that he works little and guards against excessive consumption of drink and food, and against too loud laughing
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And if he follows this instruction, he will be entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I shall tell hereafter the treatment of cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	"de la routure du ventre"
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When wounds come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow any further, then make a cautery with the cautery rope according to its quantity, and burn one-third of it near the heart
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after treating according to what we have said
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with the cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the beginning of the fistula and draw a line along its width above the fistula, and another below it, and then carefully perform the cautery incision.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cautery is lighter and gentler.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of past pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, either from falling or being struck, and that pain lasts a long time, and medical treatments are ineffective, then it should be cauterized with the cautery called 'point', and the cautery should be applied according to the length of the limb, its smallness, weakness, power, location, and twistings, and the severity of the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is without the first cautery, so much the better;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If that name, recommence another cautery on top of it, for such is the custom that it should move to the limb that is nearby; therefore you must make the cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	Of bonesetting
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Some people are helped sometimes by cautery with great benefit, especially those illnesses that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you cauterize the wound, take care if the disease is at its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not spread nor remain, and you doubt that corruption will seize the whole patient, then make five cauteries on top of it:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	One at the nape, and another towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	And two on the two horns, and one behind on the little bone;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	Hold your hand so that the cautery reaches to the bone, and so that the scabs come out so that the vapors of thick humors can escape;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	And cauterize upon the mouse as it is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the swelling is spread throughout.
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	And if it is clearly perceptible, then you must cauterize it with those cauteries that we have mentioned at the head, and one cautery near to it, and two cauteries upon the spine of the neck, and six cauteries upon the spine of the back, and one large one upon the chest and another near it, and two upon each shoulder.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	And two upon the ribs, and two upon the breasts of the lungs, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	Be careful not to burn the nerves that are situated under the buttocks.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And sometimes one cautery is made upon the bone of the wrist, and another upon the bone of the stomach, and another upon the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	Know that the more cauteries you apply, the greater the benefit to the patient.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the patient feels no pain from the cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauteries be large and small according to the members and joints, as you will find them in the various ways of using irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating the place with flour of doves' feathers mixed with honey, continue treatment until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling comes to any limb and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, but it is not healed, then perform cauteries on the limb according to its size and thickness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let the cautery be somewhat deep in the flesh near the heart;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes one performs cautery on the hand and foot and back at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus if the swelling is removed;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	but nonetheless let no one meddle therein unless he knows well the limbs and the exits of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	"of Albarus"
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the illness called 'albaras' has progressed and medical remedies are of no avail, then cauterize it with a somewhat deep cautery according to the quantity of flesh around the heart until the blackness is removed and its color changes;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then apply a poultice of wheat flour and lentil flour mixed with rose oil, plantain leaves, donkey's blood, and almond milk, each ingredient taking up one part.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And mix everything together, tie it with a cloth, and apply it to the place until it becomes sound.
li cure de chancre par cautere	"Treatment of Chancres by Cautery"
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a cancer begins, and you see it halt, then cauterize it with a fire cautery that seems like a circle, all around the circumference of the cancer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And likewise, the wise said that one should perform cautery in the middle of the cancer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	But I do not think this is good advice, for I fear that it may cause ulceration and corruption, and I have seen this happen before;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And a more appropriate thing to do is to perform cautery around it, using the cautery called 'circular', as we have mentioned in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of swelling that cannot heal
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness called 'adubelati', and it is prolonged either because of the excessiveness that it causes or because of the weakness of the patient due to old age (that is, being too elderly), and they have a shortage of blood, or because of the time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	And you shall see it hasten to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	Then cauterize it with many small cauteries, pricking all around:
aprés le laisse ensi.	Leave it like this afterwards.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see that it is piercing all the way through the cautery, then heat the cautery which has this shape:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand on the middle of that illness called 'adubelati' until the cautery pierces the heart, and make the cautery such that the patient feels drawn towards it in such a way that the course of corruption is eased.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment, until he is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the treatment of fire with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of illness there is called 'corrodens', which is nothing other than the consumption of limbs, for it consumes them just as fire consumes dry logs.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can tolerate a cautery with fire, then heat the cauteries, both small and large, according to what is needed for the location where the disease is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	Then cauterize it on all sides until you remove all the corruption, leaving nothing of it, so that all that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for 3 days, and put on the cauterized places a poultice with oil until the burns of the fire are removed, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of hot fomentations
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if, after three days, no healthy flesh appears, then it's good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	If not, then start cauterizing again where the corruption remains.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this method has sometimes been cured with medicated ointment instead of a fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	However, the fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already mentioned the cure using medicated ointment in the section on divisions:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take what you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of warts that come on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often, at the feet, a disease called "clos" arises, which is a large, broken thing that wounds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cautery for this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 namely, fire cautery and cautery with hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery should be heated like an oven poker, made of good iron to fit the nail evenly with delicate edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	Then place it hot onto the nail and turn your hand around the nail until you reach the tip of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	Leave it like that for 3 days until it begins to discharge pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then apply a poultice of crushed wild mallows with salt, leave it overnight and the nail will fall out along with its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal the place with ointment around the flesh until it is clean.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	If they are turned away from the body, which often happens in hands and feet, you must bring a cautery of hot water.
et est en teil maniere:	And it is done in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a bronze or iron rod or an oven poker and place it on the nail and around it, that is to say, for warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the funnel on so that it encompasses all around, then put some warm water inside, and hold your hand tight, and press your hand while turning such that the edge of the funnel reaches the root of the nail, and can find the deep warm water path even to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	And let the patient endure the biting sensation of the hot water for about an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then leave it thus, and it will be uprooted entirely along with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another until you remove all those that are on the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment of trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone shakes due to coldness of the nerves, or quartan fever or others, you must perform four cauteries or five on the spine of the back, one between each spine;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cautery on the foot, and one above the stomach at the 'olive' cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	So it will stop trembling, and the saints of the cold illness will be restored.
des pustules puans	For pus-filled pustules that smell bad
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No part of the body appears more often to emit stinking pustules than those coming from corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	If when they first appear, you must perform a cautery on each head of the pimple:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A fine cauterizing iron made of myrtle wood, from which the tip is heated in fire, or from the long root of artemisia, or from the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they cauterize at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow further afterwards, but the excess from which they come is severed, and they are clean.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great flows of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the backside, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cautery of the limb, and similar things
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very difficult to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And nevertheless when this happens to someone, quickly place your two index fingers on the wound of the vein and press strongly until the blood is quieted under your fingers and no more drops come out
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then place on the fire olive oil cauteries of various sizes, both small and large, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then take one [cautery], whether large or small depending on the wound and where the artery runs, place it on that vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery there until the bleeding stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you lift your fingers from the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, so take quickly another one of the cauteries that are on fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And keep doing this one after another until the bleeding is stopped;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not burn the nerve nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And know that when blood flows from an artery, it cannot be stopped well unless it is done by one of the four ways we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	Either by cautery, or by extracting [the arrow] if it has not been treated, or by tightly tying a thread, or by applying medications that have the power to stop bleeding.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And let it be tied and bound properly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Which will bring about stopping of bleeding is tying very tightly with rags or putting hot things on top, or similar things, if it profits little or not at all.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and he does not have a doctor or medication nearby, then he should place his second finger on the vein wound as we have said, and stretch it well so that it presses firmly upon the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	And do not move the finger, but wet it with cold water often until the blood is frozen and solidified and pressed.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And make such signs beforehand as are needed for cauteries and medications.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of the surgeries of wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter all diseases for which a fire cautery or hot medicine is needed, as well as their causes and instruments and forms of cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	And I have placed this chapter from head to foot in the previous one, and I will go along the same path in this chapter so that what one wants may be found more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And before I begin this one, dear friend, it is necessary that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first one about cauteries, and therefore it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter there are often evacuations of blood when opening veins, incising abscesses, treating wounds, extracting arrows, cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	There is doubt and fear, and death comes to many
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to attempt anything foolish.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many people come seeking treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	such people come from those who tend to their illness so poorly that they die easily due to the harshness of their disease and the severity of its harm.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And one must fear these things.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And there are some who give it meaning and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not consent to those who come to you with this manner, but rather put greater care into your honor than in your desire for wealth, and do not open yourself foolishly but wisely only to those whose character you know well and whom you can take in and receive praise from.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and diagnosis in treating your patients so that health may be restored
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you attain good reputation, glory, and the memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	"Dear son, May Our Lord grant you good understanding and uprightness, and if it pleases Him to inspire you with the holy breath of His hand, Amen."
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	"I have arranged this chapter in sections for you to consider, according to what is before the chapter on cupping, which I have outlined from beginning to end, so that you may find more easily what you will need."
dou chief plein d’aigue	"full head of water"
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often occurs in children during childbirth, especially when the baby's head is constricted too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes this occurs due to a hidden cause which one does not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	 And I have never seen this disease outside of children, and it always ended in death for those I saw;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	 Therefore, it seems to me that it is worth leaving the work in such cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	 And I saw a child whose head was full of water, and each day it swelled so that he could no longer hold up his head;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	 And the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture collected under the bone above the hip, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	 And if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, then you should make a wide cut in the middle of the head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	 And let it be as long as two fingers, until the moisture flows out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	 Here is the form of the spina bifida:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture has grown more and the swelling is larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	 And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see these signs: the corners of the head turned upwards on both sides, and water jumps out when you press it with your hand from within, but it does not respond to you;
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If thou must cut into the head three cuts according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	After incision, remove all moisture forcefully.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After binding the cuts with bandages and powders, put on wine and oil, and leave it thus until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then unbind it and treat the wound with dressings and anointments. Keep the head bandaged evenly, and give the patient dry food from a moist place until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to observe where the abscess appears largest, and the gathering of water;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	For sometimes it is in front
aucune fois derrier;	Sometimes behind
aucune fois en destre;	Sometimes on the right
et aucune fois en senestre.	And sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Therefore cut where the abscess appears and the collection of water is full, cutting according to your ability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	And beware that thou dost not cut the artery
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	And the windpipe of blood, so that the patient dies from bleeding and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	de reume
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it happens to someone that they have a disease called "catarrach" in the ears or the nostril, and the disease is chronic, and treatment with medicine does not help, then the last resort is to use cauterization along with cutting the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you cover the eyes, that the patient turn his head back.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	Afterwards, rub the spot with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then have the patient twist his neck with the whole cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein lies, and its location is behind both ears, and it is rarely missed.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the locations with a point, then cut both sides with a sharp spatula two parts deep until the vein reaches the bone, and this should be done at the wide part of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see, put the spatula under the artery and cut it above, cutting also like two fingers across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, then blood flows out continuously upward.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not appear when felt, then you must measure the width of three fingers, then mark and cut until it reaches the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	And about six ounces of blood should be let out, and sometimes a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the fullness of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Then examine the wound
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it remains on the sharp bone tip, if the abscess does not drain well, then compress the wound and bind it, anointing it until it is healed.
de emigrainne	de emigrainne
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When chronic migraine comes with severe catarrh and moisture from tears, and heat in the temples, along with long-standing madness and similar things, and even though medical treatments are used, none of them help, then cut the arteries of the temples and cauterize, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is such that the patient shaves the hair from their temples and listens to the artery that opens in the temple, for it beats well there, and is rarely heard outside except in some men who are excessively cold
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is heard, then the patient presses on their neck with some cloths, then rubs the spot with a rough cloth, and applies warm water to that spot until the artery appears clearly
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Then take the spatula of which this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Then carefully cut through the skin until you reach the artery, then lift it up with tweezers, and carefully separate it from the tissues beneath each part
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	If the artery is slender, cut it with the tip of the nail clipper, then cut off that part according to the quantity of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	But if it is not severed, blood will not flow freely throughout.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw out blood for six days, up to three times;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong doubled silk thread so that decay does not reach there before the wound heals, and let the blood flow freely;
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then cut off the excess that is between the two ties at that same hour, and then, if you wish, cauterize with a knife cautery up to the bone until the head is severed;
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is the best work if the patient has no fever and is of warm temperament.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauteries are helpful in drying out moistures;
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	So they are more helpful for moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	For the extraction of arrows, it is necessary that one fills the place with old cotton and then places well-made tents upon it;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they are dislocated, they should be treated with dry medicines that cause flesh to grow, and with compresses, until they are healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the artery is severed as often as you work on it, then hasten to cover it with a cautery, or use the place of quicklime and press your hand until the bleeding stops.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	And if you do not have this (quicklime) present, then place your fist on the wound until the blood is frozen, and rinse the wound with cold water until the bleeding stops, and let it be bound as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	And it is easier and quicker in extracting the artery to cauterize the vein with this sharp cautery of two parts, but let the points be well spaced so that their heat lasts longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the material is too thin, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there must be one thick spike of space between the two knives, and then when you have indicated the two places with them, heat the iron until it comes close to the bone, and cut the vein in two places.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	And let them be kept apart between the two shoulders, for it is not entirely suited to this cautery altogether.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	This is the form of the cautery
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the eyes descend from the veins that are above the forehead on the head, and it does not help to apply medication there, and you see the face of the sick person reddening, and feel tremors on the forehead like shivering
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and the eyes are thin and moist so that the hairs of the eyelashes have fallen out, and the eyelids are heated and burned by the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "treatment for contusion", and this is what you should do to the person who has this illness: let them have hairs on their forehead, then make three incisions equally spaced according to the length of the forehead
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and let one of the incisions be just like two fingers wide all around the forehead going downwards until reaching the nose, and let the other two be on either side of the eyelids above them, but beware of cutting into the arteries that are on both sides above the eyelids
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	And keep your hand away from the continuity of the two lower jaws, let each wound be the quantity of three fingers wide across the join.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	And have ready a piece of sponge and many cloths to wipe away the blood, then insert the spatula two parts from this point: here is the form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	From the incision that runs from the temple to the second incision.
