et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	And peel off all the flesh that is between the two incisions up to where the sinew is on the bone, then do likewise from the middle incision up to the other second one, and then remove this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you insert the tool called "cultellarium" into the first slit, it is very sharp on one side and not sharp on the other side. This is its shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the thin blade towards the flesh near the heart, and the blunt blade towards the bone, and press until it reaches the middle fissure.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes until the incision is continuous up to those that open from the heart, and then do likewise in the middle furrow up to the other opening.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	Then remove blood evenly, and press the area for blood collection.
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	Then place in each furrow a wisp of old cotton, and put moist cloths soaked in wine, oil, and rose water on top, ensuring no abscesses come.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	On the third day, untie the linen and apply abundant cold water, then treat with basilicon ointment with rose oil, and other treatments for wounds until healed.
dou reume des eulz	This is an extract from "Le Grand Chirurgie" by Guy de Chauliac
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	If some come with catarrh habitually, and you see the eyes thin and small, and weakened sight, and burnt papers;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hair falls out, and deep in the head there is a burning pain, and the patient sneezes.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	Then know by these accidents that those matters and that catarrh come only from many veins, and the proper remedy for it is this.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And have the patient lie on their back, then make a long incision down the middle of the forehead, and another across its width.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And begin from the left temple to the right temple, with the incision reaching down to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move during chewing.
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	And when the bone is uncovered, wipe away all the blood with a sponge, and then open the two lips of the wound and put in cotton wool and strips of linen.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then place compresses soaked in wine and oil on top, and guard against a hot abscess.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	When it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow, then dress it with drying agents that prevent inflammation of the flesh.
En teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of colophony, and make a poultice;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	And apply this to wounds to prevent inflammation throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Chapter: "The Stopping of the Ears"
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Everything that falls into the ears is one of four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	either grain, or beast, or a pebble or similar thing such as iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or seed, such as peas, beans, peas
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or flowing things like water and vinegar and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When something like a stone falls into the ear or in some other manner that does not fit with the ear and does not grow within it, then place the ear to the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, then apply a drop of violet oil or sesame oil, then perform extraction;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and when the sneezing begins, and block his nostrils as it comes on, and put around the ear compresses of cloth or wool;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	And they hold the ear above.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Often fire comes from this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	If it does not come to a head, use small forceps for extraction; here is the form:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it bursts open with the forceps, that's good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	If not, then use small forceps with a doubled-over blade;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	And if it still doesn't come out, make a hole with a needle and insert the end of the hole into the ear opening with force, then plug what is around the hole with soft wax so that air cannot enter through the hole;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	Then draw fire strongly, for often it comes out as we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	And if it still does not come out in this way, then take some glue that birds use, and put some on an instrument that is pointed for this purpose, and put some cotton around it;
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	Then press the glue onto the stone or whatever it may be, and draw fire.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it does not come from all these things that we have said, then hurry to cut the ear before the boil becomes hot and causes spasm;
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	And the manner of cutting is such that first you make the patient lie down on his back, and draw out blood according to their strength, then have the patient sit between your hands, turn the ear upwards, and make a small cut at the root of the ear where it hangs.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	Make the cut like a crescent moon until you reach the stone, then extract it according to your strength and quickly suck it into your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And continue this treatment until they are healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if it is a grain that is inside and it becomes swollen, then administer extraction.
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	And if it cannot come out, then administer the thin and subtle spatulum according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	And help incise that boil.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not do this when you think that the grain is moist due to the moisture of the ear until you have made many attempts;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	Then extract with delicate forceps and tweezers, as we have said, so that the extraction is aligned.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	Therefore, in the case of water entering the ear, the patient should first sneeze forcefully and plug the ear with soft cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And lie down on the same ear where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it flows out by itself, that's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, then take many pins according to the length of your thin fingers, and heat them a little in the fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	And have the patient insert one or two of these pins into their ear piercing through to the other side, and then pierce another pin on top of the one in the ear;
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	And continue doing this with one pin after another until all the water flows out, and thus it will all flow out;
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	And if you wish, take a reed, insert one end into the ear and hold the other end in fire until it chars;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then repeat this with other reeds until all the water flows out, as we have said earlier.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In extracting a small creature like a flea or similar, treat it as we have said in the section on dividing;
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	But if it [the dislocation] is of great size so that one can feel it, then bring forth an extraction with pincers.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	And this is the easiest thing to remove that exists within the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	When extracting worms that are inside the ears, if you treat them as we have described in the division and treatment of distillations, but the treatment does not help, then you must examine the ear in sunlight:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If no worms appear, then take them out with delicate pincers; if they do not appear, then use the tube that is depicted here:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And let it be narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And insert its most subtle end into the ear according to the extent of the patient's suffering, then suck strongly through the entire tube;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Do this often until all the worms come out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not obey coming out, then stuff cotton around the tube as I have described in the stone treatment;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	And if they still do not come out as we have described, then bring forth distillations that the ancients have proven in the killing of worms; you will find them in the treatment of distillations.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	And then distill your oil and medicines onto this instrument, as shown here:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And let it be of silver or fine brass underneath with small holes, and above for distillation;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to press during distillation, have ready an instrument of well-made brass for this purpose; and if you wish, take a razor and wrap cotton around its point neatly;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice into the funnel, along with whatever medicine you wish to use; and place the funnel in the ear;
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then insert the razor with all its cotton into the ear, pressing your hand gently until the oil is distilled cleanly from it;
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	And when the patient feels it inside, the distillation should be placed in a heated vessel over the fire before being distilled into the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	But guard against it being too cold, for then the medicine would not be effective.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Chapter: "The Stopping of the Ears"
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born without any holes in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	And this same thing happens to people due to impacted wounds or a birthmark inside the ear, and these impacts sometimes penetrate deep into the ear so that one cannot see them.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	Sometimes it happens that there is no opening and none can be seen.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	Therefore, if one cannot see it because it has penetrated deep, it is difficult to treat in many cases. But if it can be seen, you must put the ear of the patient to the sun.
et regarde dedens:	And look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	If you see the operation clearly, then perform all this procedure for which these are the forms:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And let it be sharp and cutting both before and behind, so that it does not wound the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	If the operation is a birthmark or on the flesh of the ear, then hold it with fine forceps and cut it lightly until all that flesh is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the operations are deeply embedded in the ear, then take a light and fine razor and heat it slightly on the fire, then place it on the body of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the operation from which the patient feels pain in hearing, pierce it lightly, but be careful not to damage the nerves of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	Then place in the ear a plug according to the width of the opening, and use Egyptian ointment for the dressing.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do this several days until the wound is healed, or take a plug and use rosewater for moistening, and sprinkle powdered vitriol upon it.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And if you see the ear swollen, then remove the plug and insert another plug moistened in wax made of rose oil and beeswax, until the swelling is gone.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then continue treating it until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	"And if there is discharge of blood, take a sponge and wring it out in cold water, then place it on the ear. Use other remedies that stop the discharge of blood, which are found in treatises on distillations."
de la char des papieres	"What is written on the paper"
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This substance that comes on papers from the eyes when they are moist and then dry, you should stretch it out using tweezers and pinchers, and scrape it off with a spathula from its roots.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	Then place powdered vitriol on the wound.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if it does not heal, then cauterize it with a subtle lenticular cautery, and after the incision, the cauterization should be moved.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	And many times they grow back, when some things remain at their roots;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	And when they are burned with fire, those roots are singed and do not return.
de la gresle	"Hailstorm"
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Often come onto the eyes certain things that resemble hail in shape and hardness, and therefore this illness is called 'hail', being a gathering of thick moisture on the paper above and below;
li ovraiges est telz:	The works are such:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Be aware if hail moves from one side to another; this is an easy thing to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Then make the cut wide, then scrape each part lightly, then grasp it with tweezers and pluck.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	If you cannot pluck it without piercing the paper a little, do not worry about the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	And if the crack is large, sew it together and care for it until it is healed;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if it is small, do not put any pressure on it, because the eye will restore it quickly and leave flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the hailstone descends inside the ear towards the upper part, it turns the paper, and they take the hailstone with tweezers, pressing and holding it on both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	And if the paper is moved by the incision, it matters not.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	Once the hailstone has been cut out, rinse the wound with salt water and cleanse it with material that draws moisture until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	Here's a possible translation for "de la graisse des eulz":
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a fatty substance found in the tissues of paper that affects more often children than adults, causing great pain to their eyes. In the mornings they have catarrh and cannot look at sunlight because tears rush to their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And because of this they constantly lie on their faces and sleep that way. Their papers are moist underneath their eyebrows, causing swelling and redness covered with the exinach that opens into the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press hard with your two hands and feel the exit between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the manner of working is thus: the patient places their head on your hand;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	And then take a linen cloth and prepare a tent in the shape of a circle according to the quantity that each part can contain, then place it on them;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your two thumbs on either side so that the veins are gathered within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then make in the middle of the moisture with the sharp scalpel a slit no wider than the wound made for bloodletting;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	And cut through the skin deeply until you reach the vein;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and in several positions blood comes out from the slit, resembling a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	So draw it out all at once with a wad of cloth held between your fingers, and twist your hand back and forth until it is dispersed;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	And make sure you do not insert anything into the slit lest you draw out the scalpel completely up to its eye without cutting.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the exit does not open at the beginning of the wound, then slightly pull apart the wound lightly until it opens.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then extract it as we have said, then wet cloths in hot water and cold water, place them on the wound, and press with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And there are some men who grind salt and put it on to corrupt that moisture which remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him until he is healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if a hot abscess forms, then treat it with poultices until it is healed.
des poilz des papieres	hairs from the papers
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs growing adjacent to each other in paper skin are wrapped around and become entwined, they harm the eyes and cause diseases such as habitual tears and softening of the eyelids and whitening of the eye; this can lead to blindness.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	And there are four methods of treatment:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	Either by fire cautery together, or by hot medicine according to what is written in the cautery chapter, and it is done either by incision and suturing or by ligatures, depending on what I will say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	First, place the patient's head in your lap, then turn back the eyelid with your left hand.
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	If it has turned, then that's good
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	If not, stick an needle into all of its threads
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and let it be near the edge of the paper where the hairs grow near these hairs; and draw the thread upwards over all the paper, and turn it towards the razor.
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	then cut into the part beneath the paper, underneath the hairs attached, from the large ring up to the small one
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	then pull out the thread, and place underneath the paper a small tent of cotton and cloth; then press upon the paper with an iron shaped like a bellows, like a minting hammer, but always ensure that the shape corresponds to how much you want to elevate the cut surface
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if cutting off a large quantity of paper is needed according to its softness;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	then cut along the entire spatula on both lines you have marked out, starting from the large ring down to the small one
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	And let one of the incisions be near the natural hairs in the thickness of a root, then place the cautery in one of the two angles of the heart, and then scrape it all.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	Then bring the two lips together with a stitch of thread made of fine wool, wipe away the blood, and make the excess hairs adhere to both eyebrows using any sticky substance you see fit.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	And if not, do not worry about it; then leave the stitch and the threads for three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	Then dress the wound without stitching with drying and constricting substances, for paper causes wounds to relive and prevents their healing; but stitches are harmful (as the ancients said), so perform these actions without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	And if there is another method:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	 namely: you should mark the paper with a figure resembling the shape of a myrtle leaf, as we have described, using three cauteries arranged according to the form shown here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	"Then cut that which is above the small forces equally according to the shape shown below:"
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you lack power to hold the tweezers, and the thing is not even, then take a needle with thread attached, and insert it into the figure.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and place the other thread near the large pupil, and the second thread near the small one, and bring both threads together evenly between your two fingers.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then lift your hand evenly and lift all the skin where you have cut, as we have described, then bring together the two lips of the wound with stitching, and heal it until it is sound.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	And if an abscess forms at your incision, soothe it with cerate and similar softening ointments
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and sometimes the hairs of the paper are curled
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	then you must use what we have said about incising
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but stitching is more skillful in one way and another.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of cankers is according to this form
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and it is that you fold the paper and make an incision inside according to what I have said, then make two artificial cankers and two thin ligatures as long as the paper and the width of the spathule
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	And cut both heads of both parts where you hold the threads.
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	Then gently bring together both parts onto what lies above the oil paper, and strongly pull on the two canines of both parts.
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	And let it remain thus for several days, and the hide that is pulled will die and shrink and rot until it falls off.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it takes too long, then cut it with force, then cure it so that it heals without any infection.
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	And when the wound is healed, and if the paper has been removed, the hairs will no longer point.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is how you should shape the two canines according to this figure, and according to these measurements of length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The procedure is as follows: take a fine needle and insert one thin, soft silk thread.
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then bring together the heads and tie them both gently, and let the length of the threads be a palm's width.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then prepare another fine thread of silk briefly, and tie the heads of the two threads together.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then have the patient place their head in your hand.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And let them be near the sun so that the work is well-lit, for this is subtle and delicate work. Then insert the needle all along the thread at the root of the hair and make it pierce through a piece of paper swiftly until you draw it up above the natural hair.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then pull out the hair along with the thread, and insert that hair into the thread if there is one or two or three or more;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then withdraw your hand so that all the hairs come out along with the paper and the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the thread is pulled and the hairs do not come out with it, then pull the thread from below along all the thread that you have prepared until the thread comes out of its hole and you can see it with your eye.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Then you shall draw out the dart and thread, close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hairs stand upright in their place and flesh grows over.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are short, then accompany them with one long hair from the eyebrows, and lift it up along with it, until it is lengthened and then remove it.
de la porriture de l’oil	"Treatment of eye inflammation"
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease called "aleacrati" or decay comes to the eye, there are two ways to treat it:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One is natural and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it happens suddenly from a wound, or from cutting or cauterizing, and from similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the manner of treating it is to cut open that suture, spread open the lips of it, and place linen wicks inside, allowing them to remain until the wound is healed;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	It is not necessary to use things that dry out and constrict in its treatment.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the disease will return worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	But there are things that soften it, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	And rosewater or altered and linseed oil should be cooked, and diacylglycerol melted in some of the oils, and wrapped in a tent, for eye treatment.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And your remedy's treasure is that you take care it does not heal crookedly as before.
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	These works we have spoken of are only remedies for this disease, so that it does not return in the same form as before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the flesh that comes into the oil
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This illness that is underneath, which is truly called "axacrati", is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident comes from wound and tear and cautery and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	And the way of the operation in it is that you take a needle with a doubled thread, stick it into the flesh, and make it pierce from the left eyelid towards the right one until the threads come out on both sides of the flesh.
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then stretch the flesh above the whole needle and cut it with a wide-spatula scalpel.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the shape of the paper returns as it should be, that is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If not, then take the razor and place it in the crevice, turn the paper, and make two creases on either side within the paper.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	And let the heads of the two creases be at the two corners of the incision that you have made, and form an angle such that when they are brought together, the figure is like the figure of the Greek letter "Γ".
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	Then remove that piece of skin according to the size of its sides and underneath from what is attached to the paper, then join the two separated parts together with a thread of wool.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then perform the treatment for that which we have said concerning softening medications and dressings, until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from a cut or stitch or burn, then you must make a full-thickness incision below the hairs of the paper, as described above.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then separate between the two leaves of a dressing, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And one should perform the work according to the form of the disease, for it is very diverse in form, and the wise master prepares every device with all his power so that he can make the form return to its natural state;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the patient himself, according to what is necessary for work and tools in various positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	of the suddenness of the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this adhesion occurs in many people such that the paper above is stuck with the white of the eye, and cannot move or perform its natural tasks, then you must place the point of a razor underneath the paper and lift it upwards;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	And stretch it like tweezers until you grasp what is adhering to the eyeball, which should not be too blunt nor too sharp so that the patient cannot bear if the spatula is too blunt or blinds the eye;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	And your incision, with which you remove this adhesion, should be light so that the paper returns to its natural form.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and all those gathered are healed; sometimes they apply salty water to the eye and rinse with fresh water and collyrium.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place a linen tent between the paper and the eye, and put on the eye wool soaked in egg white;
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after the third day apply collyrium and compresses until they are healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	Of the angle of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	You should know that a nail has two forms:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	one is nerve-like and similar to hard fat, and another that is not nerve-like but resembles moist snow, which when touched with iron cannot be grasped with pincers.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and both forms begin near the large pupil and gradually grow until they cover the entire sight, light, and motion of the eye.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of incision is as follows: the patient should put their head in your hand, then open their eyes;
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	Then lift the paper to your hand, then file the fingernail like tweezers of small thickness, and stretch it upwards.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and put on it a horsehair, or cowhair, or ox hair, then draw the thread tightly;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	And double the point of the needle slightly and insert it into the fingernail, then push it all the way through, and tie the nail with a thread and stretch it upwards, and scrape off all the hair on the side of the nail that touches the cuticle and the skin along the hair up to the tip, then trim the remaining part at the root of the nail bed with a sharp small scissors, leaving the natural flesh in the nail bed so that tears do not flow as usual through the incision;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	And sometimes stretch the nail only with tweezers and thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then scrape it with a sharp blade all along here is the shape:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And ensure that the scalpel does not touch the delicate tissue and tear it, nor is the probe pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	After incision, apply a drop of ground sel to the wound, and cover it with a plaster made of lead, leaving it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it as necessary until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	If the nail is not nerveless and you cannot insert the needle, nor can tweezers grasp it, many times this type of nail is cured by medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	And they grow as I have described in the division; if you wish to cover it, then open the patient's eye gently with a scalpel held thus:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	Raise the nail gently upwards; if you see that it does not thin and the reason presses against it, then distill from your mouth onto the eye a plaster made of lead and red plaster and ground sel, and stopper the eye until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	Then resume the other work according to this same operation until it is completely finished.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If there is any obstacle in the eye that prevents you from operating, such as a hot aposteme, then use milk first and cure the hot aposteme until it is healed; then recommence the operation as before until it is healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh around the eyelid harms the eye greatly, then suspend it with an onion, and cut off part of it, not all, so that no onion juice comes.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then drip into the eye red collyrium made from lead ore.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	And about the flesh that grows on the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Sometimes in the eyes of certain men red flesh is born, which covers the pupil and restrains upon the papers and turns towards the back, resembling a ruby.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the operation is that the patient puts his head in your hand, then opens his eyes wide, and you scrape off all that flesh with suitable lancets, and hold it with pressure.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then cut off the first piece of flesh, and keep cutting right down to the end without wounding the eye during the operation.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the incision of the pimple be like that which we have said in the cutting of the nail and small forces with which one removes thorns, as depicted after this chapter.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the incision is complete and all the flesh has been removed, then apply to the eye some crushed willow bark or distilled red collyrium and similar corrosive medicines, and place on the eye hot cotton with egg yolk so that it is securely covered by the abscess.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	And if there remains any residue, and hot blood overflows, and you suspect a hot abscess, then leave the eye alone and treat the abscess with cooling remedies.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work until it is clean, and so do in all cases where flesh adheres to the eye due to this cause.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But nonetheless, you should adjust the treatment of each weak eye according to its natural tendency;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and also considering accidental causes, specifically those involving iron.
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	And do not attempt any of these procedures unless you see that the patient's limbs are able to withstand them.
des voines des eulz	And about the veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Before veins appear red which cover the eye, they obscure sight and weaken the eye every day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	It is therefore necessary for you first to examine whether the eye with bone protruding from it is actually foreign, and if there is no other external disease besides the protruding bone;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	Then heat it in such a way:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Command the patient to put their head in your hand, then press those veins gently according to your wisdom, and let the onions be finely chopped as follows:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And hold two tweezers by degrees on one body according to this shape:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	Then heat it with force those veins gently, and squeeze out blood hour by hour afterward, until you see the veins swell up.
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And be careful not to cut the eye with the tips of the tweezers, and perform this task at midday before the sun, and be very thorough in your work so that you only touch those veins.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, then distill green and red collyrium into the eye to dissolve what remains of the stone.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you are unable to remove all of it in that hour, then apply a plaster made of soothing substances for the pain of the eyes, and leave it on for several days until the pain is eased and a hot abscess is assured, then resume according to this method until they are healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And these are the forms of the remedies:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the fistula of the eye
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The physicians call a fistulous ulcer 'arissati':
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you treat it with cautery and hot medicine according to what I have said earlier, but it is not yet healed, then there is a trick in it that you should incise above the abscess where it must burst, and remove all the moisture that is there until the bone is uncovered.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is uncovered, and you see the corruption and blackness, then remove everything with the instrument mentioned here is its form;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	And it is called 'sharp head', and let it be made of iron from the hammer's head, and be pointed like a file as it is in this form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it on the location of the corrupted bone, then twist it between your fingers, and press your hand a little until you know that the corruption has been removed;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this several times, then apply drying medicines.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the place is solid, and flesh is born there, and the bone of the bow is solid, and remains thus for 40 days, and it does not renew itself nor becomes an abscess, and no bad accident occurs, know that it is healthy;
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, then there is no other option but to bring the fistula back to the opening of the nose according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and that you uncover the bone again with iron and hot medicines; and when it is uncovered, then take iron number one according to this form, and make the head of the iron three-angled, and thin the stake up to its top as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	then place it on the bone near the eyelid and keep your hand away from the eye, then turn the stake entirely until it pierces the bone; the patient will feel this through their nostril if they hold their hand over it.
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	And then restore the place with dry medicines as I have taught you, and when the flesh grows and hardens the joints, then the matter goes to the sinews.
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it is easier for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	About the issue of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eyes open wide in every direction and nothing obstructs the breath nor decreases it, then you must tie down the patient;
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	Then wash it, then place cupping glasses or leeches without striking to suck, then put on the eye a linen cloth made of acacia and aloe and incense and nard, and then compress the eye, covering it with bandages and cloths;
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	And the manner of the bandages is that you take soft cloths and fold each one into four, then place them on top of each other according to how much the eye needs;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	Then compress it with a tight bandage from above and restart the cupping glasses to suck without striking.
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	Then remove the cupping glasses and keep the eye restrained day and night, and if the ligature becomes moistened, then you must draw it out carefully.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	Then remove the ligature after the day and night, and if you see the eye recovering, that is good;
se ce non;	If not
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	then recommence the emplacement and dressings and the ligature and cupping glasses until it is sound.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	About the bursting of an ocular vein
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruption occurs in the ocular tissue, then appear, and come fire from the papers like grains of resin, and it is frightening to see
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you wish to cover it, the operation is such that you thrust a needle into the root of the part beneath until it reaches that above, then thrust another needle where there is the doubled thread of the eyelid
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and make it pierce, and leave the first needle according to the direction
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cover the place of the doubled thread and tie one part of the uve around it, and bind it tightly, then remove the needle and place a linen cloth moistened with egg white above the eye
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	And leave it until the threads fall out with the ulcer, then heal the eye with soothing substances until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And sometimes the wound is restrained on all sides by a circle of cloth until it heals.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eye shows great appearance, then pierce it with a subtle spatula that comes from deep within the eye, and remove the moistened albuginea and let the eye descend and enter quickly.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then extract it until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	About the brow of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease called 'alcunnati' is nothing but bowels assembled in the eye, resembling descending water, and it is not water.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	And the manner of appearance for this operation is that you make the patient sit on an appropriate and straight seat, then take their head between your hands on both sides, and move it until you see the bowel rising up to your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	Then let it be inserted, and do not descend, nor let light enter, until the patient sees things as they were.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	And if it does not descend from below, know that it is acute; and if the descent of the bowel is not as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	Then seat the patient between your hands and take a fine spatula and cut through the corneal tissue about one point along the continuity of the conjunctiva with the cornea and the crown until the bowel emerges
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And once it has emerged, then distill hot water mixed with honey, or water in which fenugreek has been boiled and mixed with honey onto it; then cleanse it with another cure until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	Water of the eye
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have shown the likeness of acute cases in division, and what is needed for piercing
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	If done according to the instructions.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	The patient must be seated between your crossed hands, away from sunlight; keep the healthy eye tightly closed.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then place the paper on your left hand if the eye is left, or on your right hand if it is right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take in your right hand, if the eye is left, the instrument called "almagda", or in your left hand, if the eye is right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the instrument near the cornea on the thickness of a ray at the part where the lesser eyelid meets, then gently push the instrument called "almagda" until it pierces into the eyelid and you feel that "almagda" reaches the empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	And it is necessary that the measure of the path of "almagda" be equal to the depth of the space from the pupil to the end of the iris.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	And this is the cornea of the eye.
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	Then you will see the bone through the transparency of the corneal tissue, and then move the instrument until it reaches where the water is present, and then press down along one pathway after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If water flows downwards now, then the patient sees before him and the instrument in his eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After resting for a short time, if the water rises up through the second passage, place the funnel with the instrument; and once it is inserted and no longer rises, gently withdraw the sponge by turning your hand bit by bit.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then put back into water a little of precious stone dust, and lift it off from there the eye inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Next, place over the eye a plug of linen moistened in rose oil and egg yolk, and tie it with the healthy eye.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	Nowadays, we put crushed cinnamon on top with plenty of egg yolks.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if almagda cannot enter the eye because of its hardness, for there are some men who have very hard eyes, then you must take the instrument called "alberit", of which this is the form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And then carefully pierce only the connective tissue, not going too deep but making a subtle cut, then insert the sponge as we have said;
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and upon completion of the procedure prepare for the patient a comfortable resting place where he can lie on his back in a dark and quiet location;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and let him be kept free from all movement, and have light foods, and not move his head either to the right or left; and let him be bound according to his condition for three days.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then release him in that same dark room, and test his sight; and if he can see some things, then let him remain bound for seven days.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	And it is not necessary that you do this during the hour of cauterization or afterwards when incising; but rather, you should ease off on this, for water rises quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	If an abscess forms that has not burst by the seventh day, then you should open it before the eye and use a plaster that draws out inflammation.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	And when it is healed, then remove the bandage and put on its face a lint covered with olive oil to cover for several days, and keep it always in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	Then gradually leave the house little by little, and change into his clothes.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	And know that no disciples should meddle in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us from Iraq who told us that in their land they make an ointment called "almagda," with which water can be sucked up, but nevertheless I have never seen any of it in our land nor do I know if it exists in the books of the ancients.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And perhaps it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the likenesses of Almagest forms, so that those who do not know them may see them;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and they should be made of pure gold:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en .iij. angles ague.	"And their heads of these same subtlety are two, and one behind has three angles."
de la char sor le neis	To remove flesh from the nostrils
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Sometimes joined wagons are born with various shapes, among which some resemble many-legged scorpions;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	And there are those where the enchanted flesh has a rusty color, and also soft flesh with good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	Therefore, in that wagon which is soft and not enchanted, you should make the patient sit between your hands facing the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and open his nostrils, and cast the unicorn upon those wagons, and draw them forth.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	For cut off that which you can sustain on the subtle needle's sharp point until you know that all the flesh is removed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there remains anything which cannot be cut off, then open it with all the subtle and light instruments, so that nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	And if blood overflows, or a boil bursts, then burn it as necessary.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	And if it is malignant boils, then hurry and cauterize until the blood is stanched and all the flesh is burned off, then apply neat asphalt and vinegar or wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the nosebleed continues and moisture reaches the palate, know that it is healthy;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if moisture does not reach as it should, know that there is flesh grown into the bone above, to which the instrument cannot cut:
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	Therefore you must insert a somewhat thick linen thread there, moistened with hot water, and have space between each knot of at least one finger or less;
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	And the patient places the head of the thread in their nostril with some force and pulls it out smelling until it comes through the nostril into the mouth;
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	And many times children do this at school, and it is an easy thing for those who wish to do it;
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	Then grasp the head that comes through the knee with one hand, and the other head that comes through the mouth with the other hand, and pull them alternately as we do who are experienced in this.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this until you know that the nerves have rotted that flesh, then pull out the threads, squeeze out the blood, and wet the thread in Egyptian oil, and replace it in the knee as before;
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, until the oil has rotted all remaining flesh.
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	Then place in the knee a bandage of lead for some days until it is healed, and if there is need for drying medicines, use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	And this is the form of the instrument used to purge the head, into which oils and medicines are distilled for the knee:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And let it be made of silver or brass, resembling an open lamp like a tube, with its channel as well.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	And if you see [that] make a closed cane, and let the instrument be full to purge the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	And have many hands at the head to hold it when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	To remove flesh from the nostrils
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Often at the head, near the eyes, a disease called 'telul' arises, which grows and becomes large constantly, appearing visible to see.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And therefore you should cut it at the beginning, remove all hair, then put on the cautery or burning medicine in place.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	But if it is delayed to cut until it becomes large, take care whether it is hard, of dark color, and lacking sensation:
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	If you do not touch it with iron for it is an enchanted abscess; because when it is cut open, great harm comes to the patient.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	But if the abscess is soft to touch, not dark colored, and you see that it can be completely cut open, then drain the patient and cut without fear, and cure the area with drying and astringent things.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	When the nostril is cut and cauterized
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when solutions of continuity occur in one of these cartilages, they profit little, whether in some men.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	It is therefore necessary, when this happens to anyone, to consider whether the wound is fresh with all its blood.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then join the two lips together in a stitch, and continue to heal it until it is clean
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	and if the lips are already separated on both sides, you must scrape away all the corrupted parts until they heal, then join the two lips together in a stitch, and bind them tightly, and sprinkle powdered dragon's blood powder and crushed incense upon them
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put on top of the powders a strong plaster or another adhesive plaster, and leave it until it falls off by itself, then heal it with an ointment until it is clean.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The manner of stitching is as follows:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	or with needles, as we have described in the abdominal stitching;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or with thread, as I have shown you.
