puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then cut the abscess until the excess comes out, then cut the excess from the heart and leave what is tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place a cloth moistened in wine and oil upon it, then apply dressings and ointments until he is healed.
des apostemes des ners	of boils on the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Similarly, just as boils come to the artery and vein, so too do boils appear on the nerves when they are injured or from excessive exertion, etc.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens most often at shoulders and hips, and in all places where there are joints; these are the worst abscesses, their color resembles the color of flesh, and they are found in many conditions without pain;
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	And when it is squeezed strongly, the patient feels pain, but it is not deep within the body, rather beneath the heart;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	And moves easily in all directions, and does not go forward or backward, nor below nor above; and one that is in joints should not be cut with a knife:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	By chance, there might be contraction here.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And those who are at the head or forehead, cut the skin at the temple.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, grasp it with forceps and cut into its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it is large, suspend it with tweezers and scrape it off, then cut into the skin and bring together the wound edges in stitches; treat until healed.
des grosses boces pendans	of hanging warts
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes it happens in bellies and nowhere else; this is an illness called "fungus" because of its resemblance to mushrooms, having fine roots and large heads.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	There are some that are small and others very large.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	And I saw one man who had two in his belly that resembled mushrooms more than anything else; they were white with fine roots and split open, continually secreting moisture.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them open and found that one weighed eighteen ounces, and the other six; when incised, this is how you can tell if the patient is moist: the flesh appears pale, moist, and with fine roots.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	If he strikes the shoulder blade wide, and the fire cautery is present before you.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For at cutting comes many times too great flows of blood; if your blood fails, then hasten to cauterize.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	And if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-made thread of lead, and tie the artery as we have said, leaving it for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	Then bind it tightly, and do not cease to pull on the lead thread until it cuts through the artery without labor or struggle.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	And if the roots are large, then fear cutting itself for the belly, but you can nevertheless cut half of it, then cauterize so that it does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and make sure not to cut the lobe which is of fox color and poor sense and produces milk.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	"For this is an incurable tumor, and I will discuss the treatment for cancer later on."
quant li boude ist fuer	"When the wound has healed"
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the swelling of the belly comes from a cauterization of wound or cut of syphilis, and is on the belly and in some cases involves the testicles, as it happens in other diseases, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries according to what is ahead, or from flatulence;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is due to rupture of the sinew and exit of the bowel, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the flesh, and it is a light matter without pain, and has varied exits.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the bursting of the intestine, then it becomes more diverse; and when it is pressed with two fingers it sinks in and then returns, and sometimes it is hard, and greatly enlarges at the entrance of the anus during difficult labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a light thing, and opens well when you press it with your hand, without constraining [it].
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it is due to blood, then the abscess opens by these signs: large and hard, and is fixed according to a quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is due to windiness, then it is soft to the touch, and the appearance shows whether it is for arterial blood, or venous blood, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	If it is necessary for you to leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	Because there is doubt and fear about it, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is for the intestines or the bowel, then you must instruct the patient to tie their shirt and stretch out entirely straight, then press around the belly.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then have them lie quietly between your hands, then go around the place you marked with the spatula, then stretch half of the abscess upwards with the whole large thumb.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then tie around it with a strong thread or silk cord tightly, and let the knot be secure.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Then open half of the boil extended over the bandage, and insert your index finger, seeking the intestine;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you find it caught in the ligature, untie it, and place the intestines back inside the abdomen;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find the boil, take it with the pincers and cut off any excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	And if the artery or vein opposes you, go gently around it, then return to your work and take two needles, thread them with silk threads, and pierce them crosswise where you have made the incision.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then press the abscess in four places around the needles, and if it bursts, remove the needles, leave the wound to drain, and cut away any dead flesh.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	Or you can also cut it when it becomes thin and ready to burst, then treat it as necessary, and cauterize the boil as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	Extract the blood or moisture you find, then treat the place where it is necessary, and bind the joint.
dou chancre	Of a chancre
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have said in the previous section about the appearances of cancer, and how one should operate there with medicines, and how to avoid iron treatment.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And we speak of cancer spreading to the marrow, and great caution is needed in its treatment, and the ancients said that when cancers are located where they can be removed like cancers that are on breasts or in the hip area, they should all be cut out at the beginning.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	And when it is large and old, do not approach it for I have never seen anyone healed from it.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	Neither has anyone else ever been healed from it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And when the operation is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, you should purge the patient of black bile once.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	Then make him fast if he has shown signs ofpletion, then place him in a good position to perform the operation;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	Then pluck your eyelashes near the cancer, and the hair from all around it, and scrape off all the bone without leaving any behind.
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And let the blood flow freely, and press well on the wound with your hand or something else; if the bleeding opposes the incision of the artery or vein, cauterize it until the bleeding stops.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply other remedies until it is healed.
de ydropisie	Of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have previously discussed in the chapter on dropsy the similarities between it and how water is gathered together, as well as the signs of each similarity and the treatment using medicines or surgery.
si est eclites soulement;	If it has only begun to swell
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	And one should not use iron in these two conditions:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	That is to say, tympanites and hydrosalpinx, for they are deadly.
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when treating this form of dropsy called "eclites" with medications and the treatment does not help, consider if the patient is weak or has another illness besides dropsy, such as coughing, diarrhea, and similar conditions.
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	If you don't touch with iron, there is doubt.
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	And if the patient is of strong virtue and has no other illness than dropsy alone and is not too young nor too old, you should act thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Lift the patient upright onto your hands, and the assistant press the belly by pushing water towards the lowest part of the back, then take the spatula (backward facing) according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let it be cut into two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	With a point, and yet not so deep that it can reach the intestines when inserted, nor can it cut.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	Then look if dropsy has entered towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	If so, you must make a cut with the scalpel III fingers wide directly below the navel.
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	And if dropsy is due to liver disease, then make your cut on the left side of the navel III fingers wide.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	And if it's due to worms, then cut on the right side, and ensure that the patient does not lie upon the incision so that the excesses do not flow towards that weak area.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	Then pierce all the hide with the instrument, remove it and raise your hand to all the space between the skin and the sinew as when skinning, to the quantity of one fingernail or around.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	Then pierce the sinew until the space comes to the empty place, and that is the location of water, then draw it out and put this instrument in its form:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it resembles a thin silver rod, made of brass or lightweight iron, with a small hole at the bottom end.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side, three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one more
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	And the head is cut like a feather, which is the shape of the incision with which scribes cut feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	At the top of the blade is the handle, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it stops now on the instrument.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	Then empty out one half or one third of it, for if you empty too much at this time by chance the patient may die from the release of his spirit due to shock, or fall unconscious, or approach death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	But emptied according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the patient's virtue signify, and his pulse.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	Then draw the instrument and hold the water, which is now retained by the heart that obstructs the opening above the spleen, as I have spoken of, that you pierce in this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	Then begin the instrument again on another day, if you see the patient enduring this, and draw out a small quantity of water.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	Do this for some days, but guard against letting too much remain at once; just a drop of water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and leave much water in him, then he will be cured by hot earth or sand, frequent sweating baths, or exposure to the sun, and he should drink.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And the cure of drying medicines until they are healthy, and cauterize upon the stomach, liver, and spleen after extracting the water, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	The section on impotence is titled "De l'estopement de la verge" which means "On the stoppage of the penis". This refers to erectile dysfunction or impotence. The text discusses the causes and treatments for this condition.
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or with a small one, or one that is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If it must be pierced promptly with a very fine needle according to this shape:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then place over the hole this subtle plug of pitch, and tie it, holding it thus for three or four days. When he wants to urinate, remove the plug, let him pass urine, then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And perhaps no plug is needed at all, for the urine that comes forth will leave it open.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those whose hole is small shall use lead plaster, as we have said, so it may widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those whose hole is not in its proper place are handicapped; for some are born with the hole at the tip of the penis, which means they cannot urinate without lifting their penis upwards.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	And they cannot ejaculate because the matter cannot reach the mouth of the urethra, and this is a serious condition.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	The method of treatment is as follows: the patient should lie on his back, then stretch the head of the penis and cut it like the quill of a feather, so that the hole falls in the middle, as it should.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And beware of excessive bleeding that often occurs; if it happens, staunch the flow with whatever can stop blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	Of the blisters of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times these swellings come to the penis, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and among them are malignant ones and benign ones;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	therefore you should take hold of them with a sharp pin, scrape and clean all, then place damp cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment on top;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply the diaphoretic ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the navel is inflamed, of foul color and smelling bad, you must apply a cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have scraped it off, and if the swelling is at the tip of the penis, with part inside the skin and part outside, then first remove the swelling that is inside;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and when it is loosened, then treat the outer part.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For if you treat them together, then the head of the penis may not be spared from being pierced, and blackness and corruption come to its tip and around it.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore cut away all that is black and corrupt, then apply the plaster made of honey and flour mixed with pomegranate peel and figs, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, then apply the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauteries help with two conditions combined:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	That is to say, for bloodletting, and for rotting flesh;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	And if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, then you should insert a lead tube into the penis and have the patient urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the skin around the head of the penis is hard and tight, which happens to those who are not circumcised or have a wound or abscess there, then you should burn it with the cautery comb until the foreskin is loosened, and relieve the pressure from the head of the penis in all directions;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	And if it is difficult to retract the foreskin, then you should burn it with the cautery spoon slightly at the head of the penis and the skin;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then carefully draw them apart, and insert a thin linen cloth dampened with cold water between them so that it does not become hard again.
de la circoncision	Et se c’est un garcon qui doit estre circoncis, si covient que tu coupes le pelz a .vi. mois, et les autres enfans a .xii. mois; et il est bon quant tu les feras circonsire quant l’enfant aura .iii. ans ou environ.
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision does not involve continuity like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	However, when we perform this procedure by choice, especially on children, it is necessary that we do the best and easiest work for healing.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice circumcision on their children because it was not part of their law, and we only have knowledge of it through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen most masters and surgeons who perform circumcisions around the glans, and through force, and with one stroke;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	but the heart may fail because there are two veins, and sometimes one above is cut off while the other below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Or if it is covered up again, there will be double pain, and during cleaning, the tip of the member may not be secure;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and during cleaning of the foreskin, sometimes the iron may slip and ruin the work, and many times they do not need cleaning afterward, as I have seen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Regarding the cleansing done by force, I have found that using a thread tied around the entire length is the best experiment because the force cuts equally well both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, cut all around in one swift motion;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	But let the threads be well wrapped around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	And the manner of the first operation should be such that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only binding the thread around the penis at first, and then you let him rest in all ways that you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then hold him straight between your hands, and hide the weights behind your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then place your hand on the penis and blow on the heart, and pull it upwards until the head of the penis is inside;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then clean it well from the impurities that are gathered there, then tie the foreskin with a double thread, then tie it below at another point;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it there with the second tying between the pouch and the index finger, and cut between the two threads, then quickly raise the heart upwards and pull the head of the penis;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	Then let blood flow little by little, for this is the treatment;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And sprinkle powder on it and on the powder lay a bandage made of cooked egg white tempered with rose water, mixed with good fresh rose oil, and let it stay overnight, and treat again until healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form for the preparation of forceps is this:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	Let the two heads be thin and sharp, and let the heads also be as large as a hazelnut, equally.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The fault of the cautery is when the heart is cut during the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, you should stretch it to your fingernail before the wound becomes inflamed;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, use forceps, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if three days pass, and what is under the penis is swollen, let it be until the inflammation subsides somewhat, and then peel it gently.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	If you move the cup as you are able, and guard from the part of the shaft, it will not harm him at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Therefore heal the wound caused by powder with the methods we have said for treating powders; if one scoops out too much from the heart and it goes upwards, there will be no harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore heal it as we have said until it is healthy again.
dou retenement de l’urine	"On the retention of urine"
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	Retention of urine is due to obstruction from stone, or blood clots, or bowel, or flesh born, or similar things, as we have said in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if urine is not released, and you see that retention is due to a stone located in the neck of the bladder, then the patient must be made to bend over on his knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And place their feet on their back, extend their belly towards the part above the back, and let the patient hold themselves down as much as they can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And then the neck of the bladder is constricted during the expression of the stone above, causing urine to be retained.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come forth as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction using all the instruments called "syringe," of which this is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	And let it be made of fine, lightweight silver, like a bird's feather;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And let the tube be one and a half palms long, and slender at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the manner of issuing urine is that you take a doubled thread, and tie at its head a pouch of wool or cotton, and insert the head of the thread into the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And cut off the excess wool and insert it up to the head of the syringe, then grease the syringe with oil or butter made from egg yolks, and have the patient sit on a chair, and raise the bladder and penis with moistened oil of olive and hot water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then gently place the syringe in the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the belly.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and the patient feels it emptying, but this should not be done in that manner unless the tube through which it goes is twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then slowly pull out the thread along with all the lint, and let the urine follow the lint; then remove it completely, and let the urine flow freely.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and continue with the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and the patient feels relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	"On the diseases of the bladder"
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	"When there is erosion or blood in the bladder, or putrefaction has accumulated there, and you see that watery and medicinal substances are being discharged, then use all the instruments called a 'clepsydra', of which this is the form:"
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It has three holes:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	And the raised parts are such that the medicine's cutting should be so tight that it effectively stops the penis without any additional help, so that moisture can be drawn out and inserted when needed.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you see your medications entering the bladder, place the head of the funnel in the moisture, and draw out what is inside it.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	You shall draw out moisture from the cauldron, then strongly push back the lid.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	Then moisture will enter inside, and it will come to the bladder at once, so that the patient will feel it.

si est ci:	Here is
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or brass, and its head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	And below it is placed against the back where the sinews fall.
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and put into it the moisture that you wish to use for the enema, then tie it between the two breasts with a doubled good thread, and heat one part of this moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then insert the tip of the enema into the urethra, then press your hand on the bladder until all the moisture has flowed in, until the patient feels that this moisture has reached the bladder;

puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	Then insert a strong thread into these holes, then close the circle as one closes a nut, and put within it what you see of oil and moisture and water, and tie it on the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And do as you did with the bladder, squeezing by hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	"on stones"
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already said in the section on stones their types and extraction together with remedies;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	And I have said the difference between a stone entered in the kidneys, and all its signs, and in which stone one should operate by cutting;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	And in the bladder, and in the penis.
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	And I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is entered in the bladder happens more often to children, and it is a sign that water jumps from the bladder like water in its fineness.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	And it openly appears like sand, and the patient feels grit in his penis, and he often sneezes, and then becomes rigid.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	And many die from these wounds.
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	And the healing of children is easy until they are four years old; and it is very difficult in old people; and it is moderate for those between youth and old age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And treatment is easier for those with a large stone than those with a small one.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	When we come to treat, first cleanse the patient with an enema to draw out all the feces in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes hinders finding the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet and lift them up and move them downwards so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it jumps out from above.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	Then have him sit between your hands, prepared like this, with his hands under his thighs, so that the bladder is completely tilted downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	Then find it and touch it inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in the space, then quickly cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall out on touching it completely, then moisten your left index finger with oil if the patient is a child, or your middle finger if the patient is fully grown.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	And place it at its base, and seek the stone, and when you feel it with your two fingers, then move it to the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	Then press upon it with your two fingers, and push it out where you see the incision.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to extend his right hand's genitals upwards, and remove the skin that is beneath the genitals at the part where the incision is made.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then insert the spatula in place, of which this is the shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And cut between what lies between the genitals and the fundament, not midway but at the left side of the buttock.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And let it be straight upon the stone, and your two fingers always on the fundament, and make the cut across so that it is wide from without, and within narrow, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	Perhaps then press with the finger that is on the fundament, causing it to jump out without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	And know there are such stones that have corners and edges:
si est griés a issir;	If it is painful to pass:
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and some are smooth, like a pebble, and rounded, from which the outcome is favorable.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	Therefore, for those that have corners and edges, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not jump out, then you must use forceps that are shaped like a file at the tip to extract the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or place underneath the instrument a fine, curved tool at its end;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot grasp it this way, then widen the hole slightly, and if blood seeps out, sprinkle powdered vitriol on it;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there are more than one stone, first insert the largest one into the neck of the bladder, then cut it, then pull it out with forceps, and then remove the smaller ones if there are more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, it must be opened wider and a larger incision made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	If death occurs, or if urine comes repeatedly through where the wound cannot heal.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	But nevertheless, make every effort to pull out with forceps, or cut it out with pincers, bit by bit;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	And once you have completed your work, cover the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, bind it tightly, and place over it a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rose water and cold water, to cool the hot inflammation.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then have the patient rest on his neck, and do not untie the bandage for three days.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you remove the bandage, wash the wound area very well with oil and water, then apply ointment of diacereion and ointment of basilicon until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot inflammation and corruption come to the wound, and congealed blood appears in the bladder, and urine is retained in such a way that it cannot pass without pain with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Then cut your finger into the wound and remove that blood, for if it remains, it will damage the bladder and cause putrefaction.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then lift the wound of water and air and dust, and help him in all ways that you know until he is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that every time you treat him, you tie his two thighs together and gather the medications on the spot.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis, stuck within it, and urine cannot come out;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	then the treatment I mentioned earlier, which involves cutting him many times, is excused by this cure.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already tried this.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron needle according to this shape and with three points stuck into a splinter of wood
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot move back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then gently insert the probe into the penis until it reaches the stone.
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	And turn the probe in your hand against the stone little by little until you can pierce the stone on the other side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then urine will come soon after, and then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is still inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	Soon afterwards broken, and sparks fly with urine, and the patient is healed.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this due to any obstacle, then tie one thread under the stone and another above it; then insert the probe towards the stone between the two threads; then draw out the fire, untie the thread, and cleanse the blood that has gathered in the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat him until he is healed
de la piere des femmes	de la piere des femmes
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It can happen that a stone gets stuck in women, and if it does happen sometimes, the treatment is difficult, and it is forbidden for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	And the second is that it is difficult to find a skilled woman who dares to uncover herself for physicians, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third manner is that perhaps one cannot find a skilled woman in this art of hands
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth manner is that women's stones are more deeply embedded than men's, so one must make a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved. And if you must resort to this, then you should take a skilled midwife, but if you cannot find one, then seek out any discreet physician.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And she presents a well-reasoned case for the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and commands that she perform what you command regarding the inspection of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and examine very carefully whether the woman is virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she should put her thumb on the fundament and seek for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she should press it under her thumb, and advises that she put her thumb into the patient's anus, squeezing and pressing her left hand firmly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, then she must move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder until it reaches the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut on the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the anus, where it moves around and feels the stone in that area;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move her thumb above or below the stone, and let the first cut be small.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	Then place the hot iron on the hip, if you feel the stone so close the wound until the stone can exit fiery, and know that there are many kinds of stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	This is to say, small and large, sharp and blunt, long and round, and those with roots.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	and know their similarities for knowing the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood overcomes you, then place crushed vitriol in its stead, and hold it there for an hour until the blood is stanched;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work until the stone is out, and have the tools I told you about ready for extracting the stone from men to help you in your task;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if the blood overcomes you, and it is from an artery that has been cut, then place powder on the wound and bind it with bandages and cloths, and do not recommence cutting, and leave the stone alone and do not attempt to remove it, lest the patient should die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then heal the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has been stopped, and the place is ready, then return to your work until the stone is removed.
de hernie carnouse	Here is the translation of the given text with a focus on the term "hernie carnosous":
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	The gathering of water is nothing but an assembly of moisture or white phlegm that is underneath the heart of cows and contains the egg.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And it is called 'spleen', but sometimes it is properly within the tissue of the egg, so if one thinks this is the other egg.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	And it is the skin of the cow between the white spleen that we have spoken of
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	But none are like a drop of milk.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this hernia comes from weakness that affects the thighs, and this matter becomes spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	Sometimes this moisture comes from percussion on cows and has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	Either it is colored declining towards yellow, or red without blood, or black, or watery white; and there are more
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this gathering: if it is in the white spleen we have spoken of, then the abscess is round and long like the shape of an egg, and does not open the cow's skin because it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the proper cloth, then the abscess will be soft with part of the egg, and therefore one thinks it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the scrotum, he feels it well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	Therefore, when you see the color of the moisture, try the whole four-square introvert, which is shown above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	"Therefore, according to what comes after the introite, judge what is inside."
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we cauterize it with iron, the patient must be made as healthy as possible according to our ability and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then lay him on his back on something a little high, and put many blankets underneath him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on the left side of the patient, and command the assistant to sit on the right side, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs near the heart of the testicles;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the scalpel and cut the skin of the testicles midway along its length near the pubic hair, making a straight incision through the skin of the testicles up to the white scrotum, and scrape it finely according to your ability;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the sac full of water with a wide opening, and draw out all the water, then place your bandages, and let the sac be upstream.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the kidneys, but only the sac itself;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Cut it all or in pieces itself subtly, the cost of him so that if you do not cut it well enough, water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the egg jumps out during your operation, then put it back in its place once you have finished the sac's work.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then sew together the two leaves of the heart of the kidneys with a stitch, then heal it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then tie the vessels that are suspended, while doubting the flow of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the kidney with all its suspensions, and remove the egg, and heal it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if water is gathered into two parts together, know what these are";
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	Then cut the other part evenly as you did the first, then squeeze out the blood, and put on the wound clean linen moistened in rose oil";
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And put over another layer linen moistened in wine and oil, and place it on the two wounds, then put doubled cloths over them, and tie everything according to this pattern.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and fill them with woolen lint according to this likeness and sew them together at the waistband of the breeches, and one of the heads takes up the fundament as far as the back, and the other at the part of the wrist.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	And the other two heads over the two angles, and let all the restraint be assembled in the loop of the breeches.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And sometimes this root is medicated with cautery instead of iron cutting, and it is that you take one sharp scalpel cautery, and cut the skin of the wounds, and let it be heated as we have said, so that the white matter that contains water is exposed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take the cautery according to this form, and prick it once on the sinew, and burn the skin with this fine hot cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And scrape it in all ways that you can, until you scrape everything away.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and make sure the fire does not touch the eye
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	And know that this procedure is more beneficial;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And move carefully avoiding bloodletting, and gently cut as much as needed.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	If anything opposes you, such as a hot abscess or bloodletting or other issue, then treat what opposes you according to what is written above.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is afraid and will not undergo this procedure because of its horror, then prepare for perforation, as I tell you. But when you are certain through signs that we have said indicate that there is moisture there, then make the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then prick the abscess at its lower part with the entire spatula width, and insert the cautery into the wound.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	Let the opening be wide enough so that all the water flows out freely.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	Then place cotton on the wound, tie it, and let it remain for the rest of the water to flow out; then treat it until the wound is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	And if the linen bandage does not allow water to exit through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat hydrops with, whose shape is shown earlier.
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	Then widen the wound's opening and ensure that water flows out; know that six months or so after it has gathered again as before, it will then pass its days.
de l’aposteme des coions	"On boil on buttocks"
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that there is fear and many dispositions in the cutting of this vein, therefore it seems better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you about the operation and the like of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say therefore that many abscesses come into the body, especially in the groin area.
et c’est par mout de cas.	And that happens often.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is known to happen due to acidity or fever that spreads through the joints or from blows;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	And the color of the boil appears according to the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and feels no pain, yet it is a severe boil;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And sometimes there appears a painful, hard, and pockmarked boil with a reddish hue, or from the bursting of an artery or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is due to an artery, it is known by the hot disposition of the boil when pressed with two fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And one should not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	That which is caused by the swelling of a vein is known by its disposition when touched with two fingers, and it can be well incised in this manner and others.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And you should cut the skin around the joint, then pull the egg upwards and remove the fatty membrane that surrounds it.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already solid with these roots, then you must draw out the egg, along with its head.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is air in the syphilis or in those that are within the vessels, then you must remove all of this thick substance, and round off the head.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	"And if the birthmark of the skin is in the hinder part, then it is necessary that you cut off all of it and remove the boil as we have said."
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And when your procedure is completed, then fill the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then dress it with other dressings until it is healed."
de l’aposteme des coions	"On boil on buttocks"
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in wrapping like a boil, with softening of the skin, and the patient moves around crying out when touched.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment of this disease is quite frightening as well, but nonetheless we will tell you its operation according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then you place the suspensory ligature of the scrotum below your fingers, grasping all nearby vessels close to the penis, and the master ties it off firmly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then cut through the scrotum with a sharp, wide-bladed knife across the vessels until they are exposed, and then strip each side as we have described in the extraction of arteries in the temples.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then he inserts a needle where there is a doubled thread, and ties it to the first place where the wound appeared, and ties it again at the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then the edges are cut evenly straight according to the length of the body, and corrupted moisture is removed from them;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as others where one has been pierced by an arrow, so that no vessel may remain to nourish either end.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For there is no harm from this, and if blood comes from all vessels, then the ends must be drawn together on all vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the bone does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, they dry and cannot help it.
de la routure dou syfac	"Treatment for a broken nose:"
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The outcome of this treatment is through the section that extends to the side or the extension on the abdomen in the area of the groin, which causes the intestines to descend from that opening towards one end.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	And this rupture is either in the side or due to extension from it, and these two ways come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	From blows, from falls, from kicks, from lifting heavy weights, and similar causes;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And the sign that it is due to stretching of the sinews is that it happens gradually over a long time, not suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The abscesses are level with each other down towards the depths because the bowels press against them.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	"And the signs that it is a fracture of the nasal bone itself are that there is sudden pain at the onset, and there is diverse swelling apparent under the skin, due to the escape of intestinal contents through the defect in the nasal bone."
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	"And sometimes the intestines may descend with the fracture and become trapped in it, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed upon."
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	"And these fractures of the nasal bone require careful handling so that they do not happen frequently due to poor treatment."
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the manner of treating it is that you should instruct the patient to press their intestines with their hand inside the wound if possible.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then have him lie on his back between your hands and raise his thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then raise the heart above it [the wound] and cut away all the skin from the inner thigh;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert unguent-soaked bandages into the wound according to what you need to open it, so that the bone may come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then strip away the sinew that is under the skin of the thigh until all around the white tough sinew is exposed;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then insert your two index fingers into what guides the thigh bone, that which is between the white muscle that is under the skin of the thigh and between the second muscle, and separate what is behind the thigh, and between the second muscle.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And then move your right hand inside the hollow of the thighs and stretch the white muscle upwards with your left hand, and lift the thigh up towards the hip bone.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	And instruct the assistant to stretch the thigh upward and release what is behind the joint.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	Feel your two hands if there is any entrapped intestine or hard white muscle, and if you find anything, put it back into the abdomen below.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with a thick thread made of linen and insert it into the rear part of the muscle that is behind the skin of the thigh.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After the hip bone, then cut the threads that appear from the needle, until there are four left.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then they are assembled one upon the other like a cross, and tied with sinew which is beneath the skin of the testicles, with a strong tie of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the heads of the thighs and tie them firmly with two parts, so that none of the vessels nourishing them can enter inside, lest a tumor come there;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	And then place the tie according to the first tie two fingers away from it, and after these two ties leave enough sinew which is beneath the skin of the testicles for one finger's width;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and finally according to the roundness that the egg carries.
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	Then cut into the part beneath the skin of the testicles until blood flows and the bowels, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then prepare wool moistened in oil and put it on the wound, and bring the tie that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	"And sometimes it may be necessary to cauterize the exposed nasal bone after the incision has been made in case of any bleeding."
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leave the tie until it adheres by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	And if it takes time to fall asleep, let him be aroused with warm water, and apply what we have said until he falls asleep;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then heal the wound with another remedy until it is perfectly healed.
