de hernie carnouse	Here is the translation of the given text with a focus on the term "hernie carnosous":
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this art I have never seen anyone dare to perform a cure by iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like the branch that binds the wrist, in such a way that you tie the vessels lightly after cutting above gently underneath;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut into the middle of it and heal the abscess with what opens until the vessels bleed.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it as we have said until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes a fracture occurs in bones, as we have said, and the location is revealed;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	And do not leave any of the intestines at the joints, and if some are left, it's little, and repair all hours.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	And moreover if it remains too long in this state, the wound becomes inflamed or suppurated until the intestines protrude;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens due to the stretching of the sinew which is at the angles, as we have said, for it becomes stretched and then softened and swollen the joint and opened.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And its treatment is by cauterization, as we have previously stated.
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And sometimes it is cured by iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	And the patient should lie on their back between your hands; then cut the swollen area of the break with a knife, about three fingers wide.
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	And then pull out the sinew which is under the skin that follows; then take some fat and place it on the exposed area of the sinew.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And press it firmly onto the deep part of the abdomen; then sew up both visible areas of the sinew over the top of the fat, sewing one and the other.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then remove the head of the fat; do not cut into the sinew nor extend the wound or anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of intestinal prolapse.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then treat with wound care.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, cleanse it and heal the wound until it is healthy.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The infection is confined, and has no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization should be performed more gently at this place, and closer to saving the patient's life.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	Regarding the softening of the skin of the thighs
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	The skin of the scrotum is often softened in some men because the flesh inside it becomes softened; this is unpleasant to see.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	It is necessary, when one wishes to treat this condition, for the patient to lie on his back and the skin that has softened should be cut away from the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then sew the two lips together with stitches; if you wish, first sew up the excess softened skin tightly with three or four stitches.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then cut between the stitches, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed; then remove the thread.
dou chastrement	Regarding castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that those who practice sorcery are punished in our law, and therefore I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is only necessary to mention it for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	The first reason is that the physician may know how to respond when asked about it, and its treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	And the other, because we often have need of castration of certain beasts to help us, such as of goat and sheep and cat and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that castrations are done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by attraction or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one that we do by attraction, we make the beast sit in warm water until the testicles become softened and pendant;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then grasp them with your hand until they are replaced and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	On castration by cutting:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	It is necessary that you tether the beast and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspender, and cut each testicle once when they are well exposed;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave a small hole above and below where the vessels are severed;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	And this method of castration is more reliable than that done by attraction, because sometimes some part of the testicles remains with attraction, causing the beast to desire lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is sound.
des hermofrodites	Regarding hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism exists among men in two ways:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One way is that between the two testicles opens also like the form of a woman's nature, having hair and sometimes urine in the area.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And another way occurs in women: they have upon the pubic hair both like a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	The treatment for both men and women is that you cut away all adherent skin and dress it like other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, for men whose urine passes through the skin of the testicles, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	Tenting
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigine is an adherent skin on the natural part that appears too unsightly to behold;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	Some women have it as large as their hand, and this is its treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary that you shave off the excess skin of the tentigine with your hand or scissors, and then cut it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do not cut too deep, lest blood flow excessively, and then dress it like other wounds until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	And there is another wound that arises at the mouth of the womb, and the hymen, and sometimes it swells up like a cow's horn; therefore the ancients called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	It is necessary that you bind it, as we have said regarding tenting, and continue the treatment until it is healed.
de erratique	Erratique
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Incorrect if the woman's nature is not pierced, or the hole is small.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	And it is either natural by birth, or accidental due to illness that has come upon it.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	Or it is caused by adhesions of flesh, either thin or thick, and occurs deep within the womb, on the sides, below, or wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	And it prevents conception, childbirth, and sometimes menstruation as well.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	The diagnosis of this is made by examination of the belly.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the inflammation appears nearby, then seek it in your two ears or in your throat.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is due to thin adhesions, and it extends for two fingers' breadth, then hurry up and round it in this manner:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Join your two index fingers together, with the woman lying on her back and her legs spread apart;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then the two books are fully opened, so that the subtle face is rounded, and the poultices are covered.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, dampen it in oil, place it on the wound, and have the woman lie face down each day so that it cannot dry.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the shoulder blade is hard and thick, then you must cut it like a bay leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the poultice is of new flesh, then suspend it from the ox's horn and cut it off;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have ready staunching medicines such as aconite, dragon's blood, frankincense, mixed with egg yolk.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then prepare a wide lead plate so that the wound cannot dry out.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And likewise have ready a tent of dry linen.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then let him be treated with other remedies until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when flesh-born matter comes in the wound, it must be cut according to this manner, unless it is an incurable abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an incurable abscess that is in the wound, one should not cauterize with fire.
des emorroides	Emorroides est une maladie de la partie postérieure de l’anus et du périnée, causée par une dilatation veineuse ou un hémorragie de ces veines. Les symptômes incluent le saignement lors de la défécation, la douleur dans la région anale, et des masses dures à cet endroit.
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are abnormal openings of veins from which blood usually does not flow, and when hemorrhoids are old they become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And as we have said in the division, their similarities, signs, I will say here those that require treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and piles, when they are buried deep in the marrow, and they cannot be felt, then there is no cure by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the anus, which can be felt, those can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is necessary then that you place the woman in a cold house; then put hot pincers on the navel with tongs and cut it at its roots; then apply powder containing medicines that stop bleeding, such as acacia and dragon's blood incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then place her feet to the fire for an hour, then put her in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if bleeding persists, make her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and gall nuts and similar things; then take barley flour, mix it with honey and celery, and apply the plaster on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if she bleeds, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, then apply cupping glasses to her back and breasts without striking them.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take wool, wet it in plantain juice or celery juice with old wine, and apply it to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess is ripe, then treat the wound with ointment until it is clean.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And the one called 'albathir' is red, and resembles a sharp-pointed head, so it should be covered just like the thelul.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then perform treatment until he is healthy.
des apostemes de la marris	Of boils of the anus
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscess occur in the martyrdom (i.e., the genitals), such as chancre, pierced abscess, herpes, erysipelas, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in their categories.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is therefore necessary that I discuss in this treatise the hot abscess that appears in the marrow, which is not one of those that boil.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the work of iron, look whether the abscess is hard at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and becomes red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Therefore do not hurry to pierce, but let it swell until the pain subsides;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	And then have the patient sit on a chair, and place two small chairs where they can recline, and lean on their back and bring their feet together below the knee.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let their thighs be spread apart, and place their arms under their knees, and tie them securely with a good bandage;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then follows the removal of the bile towards the right side, and there one brings the instrument with which one operates the mouth of the gallbladder, about which further details come below.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you bring this instrument there, you insert the reed first to know the depth of the gallbladder, so that what enters from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not burn the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	And if the instrument is larger, then one must cover the depth of the gallbladder with rags so that the instrument does not cause pain.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	And it is necessary that he place the funnel of the instrument above and that he moisten the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens and one cuts into it with a gentle hand, then one must cover it at the head, at the upper spine.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	And when the gallbladder is emptied, then you must put in the wound wet bandages in rose oil or in dry green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	And place the hot iron of the cautery on the bottom of the wound, and put behind it a wick moistened in water where mallows have been cooked.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then, after two days of applying this ointment, continue until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	And sometimes lift the wound and the boil with an enema of water and honey, then with water where roots of lily and long aristolochia have been cooked.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	Then apply the ointment again.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is in the marrow, you must beware of cooking with iron, but treat it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	Childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is first necessary that she know the shape of natural childbirth, and the sign is when you see the woman straining downward, and wanting to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	Then the child hastens to come out.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	You then know that this birth is according to its natural form, and the head is the first to emerge, along with the afterbirth.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	When you see these signs, gently press her belly so that the child comes out quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	Because when he sits on his head, so does his second line with him, and the bridle of his excesses is cleaned by good purification;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	And that which comes differently does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	Because sometimes it comes on its feet and the body or head turns upside down, and the hands, or it comes onto its belly, often turning by chance onto its neck, and into other unnatural positions;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	Therefore it is necessary that the midwife be wise and skillful in these matters, careful to avoid error and deception, and I will show you all the positions and how to assist them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out onto its head naturally, and the woman gives birth screaming, and her strength is weak, then have her sit on a stool or let the women hold her up;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and raise her nature with oil or ground fenugreek cooked, and then put the midwife between her thighs the small spatula, of which here is the shape:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	Cut the navel cord, and clip it with nail clippers until the moisture inside flows out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	And press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must administer a suppository of ground fenugreek mixed with sesame oil to the woman;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her inhale warm steam and sneeze, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	The child will now be born.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands come out first, you must gently push them back in bit by bit;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot be pushed back in, then place the woman on a seat and raise her feet up high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then suddenly lower the seat to the ground, taking care that the woman does not fall during this maneuver;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if the hands still cannot be pushed back in and the child is dying, then cut off the hands at the joint just mentioned, extract the child, and reset it correctly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	Of the birth of a child upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes onto its feet, then you must push upwards.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn it gently, little by little, until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then grasp one of the feet and stretch it out gently.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it can jump up to its thighs, then command it to grasp [the foot], and make it sneeze with conditions.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If it were to leap, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if he cannot jump as we have said, then turn it bit by bit until it is in its natural shape
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it is easy
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come forth as we have said, then take musk-rose of old age, and sesame oil, and melted gum, and grind all in one mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	And put this ointment on the woman's womb, then make her sit in hot water up to below the ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	And when she is moistened underneath, put a collar of myrrh on her and leave it there for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	Then make her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child will leap now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the outlet of the child onto his knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When a child comes in this form, then the midwife places her hands softly and gently.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	Then let it be suspended by its neck, with its feet hanging down, lying on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold her hands gently and gently, then she takes her hands to place them on its belly, removing the pillows underneath so that it is well positioned below;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not slip out, she takes its feet and pulls firmly, then brings her belly upwards, and then inserts her hands;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and remove the child gently.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and tell the woman to hold herself back so that the child comes out easily.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the outlet of the child who comes from the thigh, keep one hand
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to devise a means of reducing dislocation:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be reduced, then make the woman stand up and walk around;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then make her lie down on the bed, and forcefully extend her legs;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the cataplasm that I have described
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then make her sit on a chair, and then try to reduce the dislocation
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	And wean the child according to its natural figure, and let it sneeze, and instruct her to suckle until the child is full.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the outlet of the child on his neck, with his hands spread out and his face turned towards his mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the peasant take his hand, then turn it gently and gently, and weave lightly.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is even, then apply the medicinal plaster of alum and oil, as we have said, and instruct her to move gently.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	Then make her sit on the seat, and tell her to suckle;
et la fai esternuer.	And let her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In the same manner for all the afterbirth
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When the second milk comes forth in this manner, cut off the second milk with your nail until the moisture is emptied;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	And if the child falls on its face and neck, cut off the skin from the corners so that it does not remain trapped, lest the child die;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then place the child inside until you have positioned it correctly, and instruct the woman to suckle several times:
adonques si istra legierement.	Then it is to be healed easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	From the outlet of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are often born, sometimes even three or four at a time;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not unusual, it happens quite often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are strange, and do not live long unless named early;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know them, that they multiply, and are devoured by the wolf who divides them, which is tied to the mouth.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes they come out as naturally as one all at once, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	If they are born crying, then the treatment should be carried out as we have said, and let the midwife be skilled, doing what she does quickly and easily;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so in such a way that it leads to health.
de plusors enfans	Of several children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb one or two or three or four or five or six or seven, or even more up to fifteen, and all are perfectly formed like children by the measure of the glorious Creator, and thus the midwife should know everything about this, for such things can happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	If it is done as it ought to be.
de l’enfant mort	Of a dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman for a dead child or miscarriage, as I have mentioned in the division, and it does not expel, you are compelled by necessity to act with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	Therefore, you must know if the woman is of sound virtue, and whether she has no accidents or fears death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary for the woman to be positioned on her back, with her head inclined downward, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And the helper must hold her thigh at two points, or tie it to the bed so that she cannot move during the descent of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the womb with moist oil made from althea and fenugreek and linseed, then anoint your hands with these oils and powders.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then place them gently into the womb, then seek the location where she expelled the waters that are suitable for this purpose, and be careful that if the child is presenting feet first it does not descend headfirst.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If the splinters are in his eyes or neck or mouth or throat or cheeks or under the beard or near the armpits, and if the dislodging is below the feet, he should push or pinch around the middle ribs;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And he should grasp the splinter with his right hand, place the crook between the middle fingers of his left hand, push gently with his whole hand, and insert the splinter into any of these places that we have mentioned, until it reaches its empty destination;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the splinter:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert against the other splinter, or the third one if necessary, so that the extraction is even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then pull them evenly by moving from side to side, so that they come out more easily, and the splinter should have teeth for better gripping, as shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if there remains a part of it, then he should smear some of his fingers with oil and push them into that part and pull out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if there remains none, then place this ointment at a higher location, and do so until it has all flowed out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other and cannot be brought back due to tension, then you must wrap a bandage around it until all tension is released.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then strike the handcuffs at the joint of the sole or the wrist, and likewise you must do with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is tight at the outlet, or if there is an acute angle assembled there, then you must insert the spatula spinous between your fingers, splitting the head and extracting the fluid.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or else round it with the instrument called "almidach", with which the shape comes out along with the instruments in the chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And do the same if the child has a naturally large head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	And then seize the bones with pincers, and if the head jumps forward and is restrained by the forceps, it should be cut, until the moisture in the bone socket comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces with a saw where you can reach.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	Should it be swollen in the abdomen or below the ribs, then it must be pierced until the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	"And if the child is on its feet, then traction is easy, and directing towards the mouth of the matrix is also easy."
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is tight in the belly or the wound, then you must pull it out with a cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	Open the belly or the wound until the moisture flows out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if the other bones are disjointed but the head remains in place, then insert your hand deep into the flesh and pull it up to the entrance of the socket;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then insert one or two fingers and pull it out.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the entrance of the socket is narrowed due to heat from an abscess that has formed there, then one should not work it open; instead, apply moist and greasy things.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And the plaster maker uses, and this is in softened and moistening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can make it even, then plaster as we have said in the living child:
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if there is no power, then remove it by sections, and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if the plaster as we have said in hot boils that come on the face:
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, then let it be put into tightening water, and the plaster other remedies.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman whose womb contained an infant that had died, then another infant became lodged on top of it and also died
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, she developed inflammation in her vulva which swelled so much that it opened up and began to emit a foul odor
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat her, but after pondering for a long time, I could not heal the wound
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attracting plaster and an bone emerged, then after several days another one appeared
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly astonished by this, for the womb has no bones
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I concluded that they were bones from a dead infant
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I sought the wound, and pulled out many bones, until the woman was better.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman lived a long time thus, and sometimes a little bit of bowel came out from there;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	I wrote this chapter only so that when the master finds something strange, he may know how to help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	"to bring the dislocation back into place"
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Hereafter follows the form of the pressure, by which books are weighed;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	Also, turn to page two for the heads of the ribs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	And always, let the horn be more subtle in restraining, and make it from ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the wood should be two fingers wide, and its edges one palm and a half long;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two ribs there should be two joints of this same wood, which close firmly on both ends, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two joints are placed in the mouth of the mallet to open it when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made from ebony or boxwood wood, according to the shape of pliers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	And it should have two joints at each head, as you see, one palm long and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	And when you want to open the mallet with all the instruments, then have the woman sit on a bed, feet hanging down and legs spread apart, then insert the two joints together into the mallet, and hold the head of the instrument under her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then open your hand to all the instruments, just as you have done evenly with the forceps, according to the quantity that you see opening the mouth of the abscess, until the boil does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all mounted, and their appearances are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the physician has prepared them, the work goes faster, and the higher for men because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	"Do not disdain the instrument until you have prepared it, for its necessity is not excusable."
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must command the woman to hold her breath, then make her sneeze with condition, and hold your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she sneezes because of this, all is well.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then take hot water, and make a hole or an opening, and put in herbs that can open the mouth of the abscess, such as celandine, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centory;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then place a tube through the hole of the pot and put the other end into the mouth of the patient, keeping it there until the steam enters the patient.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	"If the membranes are expelled quickly."
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains afterward and is not completely healed, command the maiden to wet her left hand in sesame oil or in ground iris and then place it on the navel, pressing gently.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she has found it, take it and stretch it little by little straightly so that the patient does not fall during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but one must move it gently to right and left, then pull gently
si venra et se desaerdra.	then it will come out and be freed.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the patient is too narrow, we have mentioned the treatment of sneezing and fumigation with herbs
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	If it does not come from any joint we have spoken of, then ensure you do not err in its treatment.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But you must tie what is at the mouth of the womb to the woman's hip, then perform a clyster with terebinth wax.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If it can be extracted and replaced, then fire will come.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	However, when it is extracted, if a bad odor comes to the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, foments suitable for this are required:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	The ancients have proven that fumes from watercress and dried figs are beneficial.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	"The shape of the instrument used to fumigate the woman during the retention of the flowers and membranes is as follows:"
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	It is like a snake's head in appearance, with the subtleties of nature placed at its top, and wide branches above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let there be fumes on the coals, and continue until the wick is spent, then begin another.
de percier lou fondement	"to pierce the anus"
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born whose anus is not open but obstructed by some subtle membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary for the woman to pierce that boil with her thumb, and not touch it with her nail, and cleanse the clothing so she does not touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place wet linen soaked in wine and oil, then treat with salve until it is healthy.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	"And if you doubt that it has not healed, then place a tube of lead in the opening and leave it there for a few days, removing it when the child is ready to be taken to its room."
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this swelling comes suddenly from a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	If it happens suddenly:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	then treat it as we have said for the boil of the buttocks.
de la fistule dou fondement	"of the fistula of the anus"
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come under the anus are nodular and growths that come near the anus or in the space of the buttocks are also considered fistulas, one or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when this nodule is chronic and grows, it emits moist white pus or subtle bowels, and sometimes these fistulas persist;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	They are recognized by those who experience emission of wind or ventosity during evacuation, and sometimes a worm jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that extend to the bladder, and halfway down the penis.
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And they reach as far as the hip joint, and as far as the buttock's point.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula that perforates the anus, but does not perforate:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and stick your two index fingers into the anus and insert a thin needle of brass or iron into the fistula where there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has tortuosity, insert a thin reed or horsehair into it until you feel the reed or hair with your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge of pus or wind or bile from the opening, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not penetrate.
si te haste dou curer.	If you hurry to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	"And when the fistula is perforating up to the bladder or up to the urethra, urine comes out of it and cannot be healed by medications."
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced as far as the hip joint, then the reed will come up to that place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twisting and the source of pain cannot be found, then it is always worse, and there is no use in applying medicine or poultice immediately.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And for these Persian fistulas, there is no cure other than labor, and the foolishness of those who meddle with them in vain.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In those that are not Persian and are not ancient, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced; and it is necessary for the patient to lie on their back between your hands.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And lift their legs up to their thighs, and let their thighs be inclined towards their belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then place an awl or a probe if there is twisting, until you know where the opening is located.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around their anus, then you must insert your two index fingers there; now you will know if the awl has pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And when you feel between your fingers either the sinew or the flesh, then know that it is a Persian fistula.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If one does not work at it, one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said everywhere that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid one does there, if it is to heat the cautery subtly according to the width of the fistula, as it is said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	And place everything hot into the fistula until it reaches the bottom;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this twice or three times until you know that these broken vessels have been burnt, which resemble an ostrich feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then use warm compresses to rub until this vessel comes out, then apply ointment inside the wound and around it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is healed thus, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If not, it cannot be healed otherwise.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if the tent enters and does not pierce all the way to the base which is at the bottom, and between your two fingers and the tent there is a thick layer of flesh or fat, then you see the fistula coming out through this fatty covering.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If you cut off the beginning of the fistula, and push it forward again, and then apply the cautery afterwards until it reaches the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	And the tent will be delivered, and it will fall.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then cleanse those shattered bones that resemble a bird's feather, and leave none remaining.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	"If the sinew breaks and tears between you and the work, cauterize it with fire or strong medicine."
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery combines two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	 namely, the burning of these joined bones and the draining of blood and drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then for wet tents in furuncles or broken skin, burn until the place is bare and the burned bone emerges from the boil;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with quick-acting oils that soften hard flesh; these are dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	"For when it is cauterized in this way, it is truly cured and does not return."
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	"And if the fistula comes right down from the fundament and is far from the body, push your thumb into the fundament and search for it."
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between two there is cloth or skin or bone where it is about to burst, then make an opening with confidence and hope by administering one of these three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	When you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it all the way down to the bottom, then insert tents there if possible and treat it first.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too deep lest you cut the tissue that holds the fundament, causing unwanted evacuations to occur there.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	Perhaps it will then be healed, or you may remove that covering and clean it after cutting near the fundament using a tent or other pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse the faulty flesh in the wound as much as possible;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study how to heal the wound and keep the fistula away from the fundament:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	So that it may be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And there are some fistulas that follow this manner
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	That is when you insert the tent into the fistula, and it is located near the fundament on the skin above, then take a pierced tent with this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	"And tie one end of a thread to the top of the tent, then insert the tent all the way into the fistula until it reaches its tip."
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it pierces the margin of the foundation within, then pull out the thread of that hole, so that you push your thumb into the foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and draw the head of the thread, and bring the two heads together, and tie them to each other, leaving it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and tighten it occasionally until the threads cut through those tissues that are between them, and lie flat.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is closed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	"If the fistula does not burst open on its own, make it do so by any means you can, unless it is too deep."
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"For it would not be good to cut too deeply and then treat it as we have described until it is healed;"
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spina bifida deformity from which a fistula is opened is usually angular, with one side concave and the other convex;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other hand it may not be, because you should not cut what you should not cut, as you can see here
des emorroydes	"hemorrhoids"
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Worms are of two kinds:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Either they are within the fundament like grains of resin, some small and others large, with blood constantly flowing from them, and there may be one or several, and they are defective in the fundament and at the head of the fundament;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those that are displaced have little moisture, and often contain a bit of yellow bile or a bit of blood, having the color of flesh.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them within the fundament is to instruct the patient to strain while walking in chambers until the haemorrhoids come out and become apparent.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	So hurry, and take it with forceps or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its root.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the forceps cannot hold them due to their moisture, take them with a cloth, cotton, or a piece of linen.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	Then pull them out with your two fingers, cut them off, and apply some warm powders in place of cauterization.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the haemorrhoid cannot come out, clusterize the patient with a biting and sharp enema to wash what is in the fundament so that it can come out clearly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient can't sit up on their own, and if the threads were fiery at their base, then the treatment is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	Then you should grasp them with your fingernail or forceps, cut them off, then cauterize them as we have said until they are clean and the incision by iron is feared.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	If it is necessary that you arrange the suturing in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread, insert it into a needle, then draw the thread upwards and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn both ends of the thread under the needle; let it be wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And pull the thread tightly, then tie the knot, remove the needle, and do likewise for all the others; leave one loose to absorb any excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the wound a moist cloth soaked in rose oil or wax, and cover it, instructing the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then let them fall until they drop, and once they have fallen, heal them with ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	"For the drying of the fissure in the fundament:"
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	"Often times a fissure occurs in the intestines due to drying, and this can happen naturally or when the patient is old and medication is ineffective."
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you scrape off the outer skin of the boil with the point of a lancet or your nail to prevent it from getting wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then heal it until it is solid as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot heal, then resume scraping more forcefully than before until it heals completely and the skin is peeled off.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal it until it is healed.
dou fremit	"For trembling:"
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A formice is a small hole made by an ant that goes very deep into the body;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes cold finds it, and he feels almost like dead from trembling, and it comes throughout the whole body, but more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment for this is that you take a feather from a goose or a strong crow's feather and place it on the trembling so that the circle covers the trembling entirely;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to the entire bone until you encircle the quivering, then place it deep and press down on the roots of the quivering.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	"And if you wish to do this with a feather of brass or iron, then do it in this manner, and make sure that it is thin underneath and sharp above:"
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Nor pierce it, so as not to hold onto both sides, or squeeze too hard.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, cauterize the quivering, as is discussed in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	"Of the form of a clyster:"
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a silver or lead enema is given, or melted copper or brass;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these small and large instruments are used, according to the person for whom they are intended.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	"Therefore, those that are used for the treatment of children and those who are weak and sickly should be small;"
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	"The form of a small or large clyster is as follows: wide where the belly is bound according to this manner:"
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is constipation or the belly is bound up, as you see, and the feces are pierced within;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and there are two perforations on one side and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and the belly should have medicine placed inside a beast's bladder or parchment pouch, pierced all around with small holes, with one inch of space between each hole. Then insert strong thread made from coarse yarn twisted into an 'X' shape or wrapped around, and tie the belly closed like a goat's udder.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, then tie it to the instrument ahead with a strong thread, then enema.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and grease the head of the enema with oil or egg white, or something similar, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister squeezes with both hands together until it is all out, then remove the enema, and the patient lifts their legs towards the bed, and if the medicine wants to come out, tie as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if he sleeps a whole night like that, it will be more helpful.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if you perform a clyster in an illness where the belly is inflamed and the medicine rushes out quickly, then repeat it until it is healed."
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are at the fundament or abscess, let the enema also be as subtle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the form of the subtle enema where the skin is stretched
des plaies	Of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already said in the division the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	I will tell you about treatments of hands and medicine, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	"I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where they are made, and what they are made with."
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	Things by which wounds are made are by blow of stone, and cut of sword or dagger, or spear or club or arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Or made according to the locations on the body, such as wounds that fall on the neck or head or buttocks or belly, or liver, and similar limbs.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and begin with simple head wounds, since the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, you should consider whether it was caused by a blow of stone or similar things, and if the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, then you may doubt hot swelling.
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	Then cleanse it quickly with the cephalic [cephalic vein] itself, especially if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the cleansing be contrary to the wounded part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And when the patient has finished his consumption of wine and fatty foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not wish to improve, then let his food be made smaller, and let him neither drink wine nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And place on the wound, if an abscess should come about, cotton soaked in oil cooked only, or in stringent wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no hot abscess, then place on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood and not moved by the air, powder that I will mention later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the air has moved it, then place on it some ointments until it is healthy.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like one from a sword cut and similar ones, and its lips cannot be brought together by binding alone, then bring them together by stitching, as I shall say regarding wounds of the belly, concerning stitches.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is open to the bone, and deep, and hangs only by a little, then cut it.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medicine, and replace hard flesh in place of skin, and instruct the patient to eat fatty foods such as testicles and cooked wheat, also poultry, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find rottenness in the skin, but it hasn't reached the bone, cut away all the rotting part and burn it with fire, then treat [the wound].
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein that cannot be stopped from bleeding with medications alone, then seek out the artery. And if you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not help, cauterize [the artery].
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is easy:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and this is what you should do: put in this powder that seals before the wound closes.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And here is how to make the powder:
pren encens une partie;	Take frankincense, one part;
sanc de dragon II parties;	Dragon's blood, two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	Grind this finely and fill the wound, binding it tightly until it is well-closed and joined with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	And then bind it well and leave it without removing [the bandage], unless it swells;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Because one does not remove medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	Sometimes heat alone is applied when incense or dragon's blood are not available, but only after the art has moved the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound has moved, especially in summer, do not apply this powder there;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some digested oils or poultices made from barley flour and water mixed with honey, until it softens.
