Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is forward, have the patient lie down, as we have described for those with dislocations of the knee, and remove the rope from the sick leg properly, and also from the foot;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two torches, one at the head and another at the feet, then insert one torch between the thighs of the patient in this manner;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And have moistened cloths ready to tie around it so that the patient does not burn, then each minister extends towards him, and the physician places his hand evenly on the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, that's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, then place upon [a] table, and press as we have said in the case of kyphosis; let the patient lie on their sound side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is before you, then quickly extend the patient's affected leg, as I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And the physician places his knee over the patient's thigh, then presses with his other hand, and extends down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is at the back, then it should not extend the patient downwards nor lift them up from the ground; rather, they should be positioned as if the hip was dislocated at the back, just like we have described for childbirth on two hips.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and they should lie face down, and the ligatures extended as we have said before, and all must press upon the joint with the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	And the condition will improve when the patient extends their legs, with them being even.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then join the thighs, place the splint, and secure it with a bandage so that the hip does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And after three or four days, remove it, then place the splint on top;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	If you see that they are even, then secure it again as before and leave it for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then remove it, and let him walk gently until the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Chapter on dislocation of the knee joint
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee can be dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, inward, outward, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	And it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	The sign is this: have the patient bend their leg towards their thigh, and if it does not reach their thigh, then know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the reduction for all of them is this: have the patient sit upright, extend their leg if they can, place your back against their face, and put their foot on yours;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take his knee in your palms, and withdraw it between your thighs, then bend both sides of the knee strongly.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And another assistant extends his foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign that it is correctly reset is when he can move his leg easily at the hip.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	Then apply the plaster on top and secure the leg to the hip with bandages, binding them tightly for three or four days, then untie it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And let the patient not walk at all until the member is healed.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	**And if the limb is not completely healed, then administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of dislocation of the hip, until it is fully set.**
de la dislocation dou talon	Chapter on dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	"The heel can sometimes be wry and sometimes completely dislocated, both inward and outward."
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	The sign that it is dislocated is when the ankle is swollen and sticks out on the side where it is dislocated.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reset should be easy, and one can easily extend the arm with their hands when it is only slightly dislocated.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is completely dislocated, then you must make the patient sit upright and have one assistant hold him firmly by the leg above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then draw the foot towards you with your right hand, then with your left hand twice, then lift it up high and place the foot well up high;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, lifting and drawing the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it returns, that's good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If not, then start again the operation, for it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it still cannot return in this way, then have the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly plant a post into the earth between their thighs, and tie the ropes around to prevent injury to the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then the ministers take hold of the thigh, and another minister extends the foot with their hands or with a rope so that it lies on the collarbone of the foot.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then each minister stretches equally, and let the post always be between the patient's thighs to hold the patient steady when lifting him.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then the doctor puts his hands equally on the dislocation, and another minister holds the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will quickly return.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it has reached its peak, then place the plaster and swabs on it, press strongly, and bind the foot to the leg, and watch carefully the nerves that are above the ankle behind, so that the binding is not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then let it be for two or three days, and if the binding loosens, then press strongly.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then untie it on the third or fourth day, and forbid walking to the patient for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if he walks before this time, there is no certainty that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"If inflammation occurs around the dislocation, you must calm it as we have described elsewhere until it is healed."
des dois	Chapter on dislocations of the fingers
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	"When the fingers are dislocated, they should be gently extended without force, which is easy to do."
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any of the joints at the back of the foot, then have the patient sit on a flat surface or on a stool completely upright, and place your foot on what opens up from these joints, then press strongly with your foot until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is aligned and nothing opens up, then place under the sole of the foot a two-legged stool, then press strongly, and let it be for three days, then untie it;
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Chapter on wounds accompanied by dislocations
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When an injury occurs with the dislocation, and it is reset, many times the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	So do not be presumptuous in the treatment unless you are wise in the art and have practiced it extensively, and if you are compassionate, merciful, and cautious, not hasty.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	And use soothing remedies for a hot abscess at the beginning, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of recovery
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	But when you do see hope, reset the limb now before the hot abscess comes
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when the limb is in place, administer remedies to cool the inflammation and treat the wound with drying ointments
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is also fracture or small bones dislocated, set them, and do as we have said in simple fractures
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And guard against entering into fear, according to what I have said, for it benefits you more to move according to your Creator, and for the salvation of your soul and body.
